italic\">\r\n                                            Volume: {meta.currTot} questтФЬ├Бes\r\n                                        </span>\r\n                                    )}\r\n                                </div>\r\n                            );\r\n                        }\r\n                    })}\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n        );\r\n    }\r\n    return null;\r\n});\r\n\r\nconst getMondayStr = (dateStr) => {\r\n    const dt = typeof dateStr === 'string' && dateStr.length === 10 && /^\\d{4}-\\d{2}-\\d{2}$/.test(dateStr)\r\n        ? new Date(`${dateStr}T12:00:00`)\r\n        : new Date(dateStr);\r\n    if (isNaN(dt.getTime())) return null;\r\n    const day = dt.getDay();\r\n    const diff = dt.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);\r\n    dt.setDate(diff);\r\n    const y = dt.getFullYear();\r\n    const m = String(dt.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');\r\n    const d = String(dt.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');\r\n    return `${y}-${m}-${d}`;\r\n};\r\n\r\nconst formatWeek = (isoString) => {\r\n    if (!isoString || typeof isoString !== 'string') return '--/--';\r\n    const [year, month, day] = isoString.split('-');\r\n    if (!year || !month || !day) return '--/--';\r\n    return `${day}/${month}`;\r\n};\r\n\r\nconst shortenLabel = (value, max = 18) => {\r\n    const text = String(value || '').trim();\r\n    if (!text) return '├Ф├З├╢';\r\n    return text.length > max ? `${text.slice(0, max - 1)}├Ф├З┬к` : text;\r\n};\r\n\r\nexport const WeeklyEvolutionView = ({\r\n    categories,\r\n    studyLogs = [],\r\n    showOnlyFocus,\r\n    focusSubjectId,\r\n    maxScore = 100,\r\n    minScore = 0,\r\n    unit = '%'\r\n}) => {\r\n    const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState('performance');\r\n    const [userToggles, setUserToggles] = useState({});\r\n    const [hoveredLine, setHoveredLine] = useState(null);\r\n\r\n    React.useEffect(() => {\r\n        // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/set-state-in-effect\r\n        setUserToggles({});\r\n    }, [showOnlyFocus, focusSubjectId]);\r\n\r\n    const categoriesSignature = useMemo(() => categories.map((cat) => {\r\n        const history = cat?.simuladoStats?.history || [];\r\n        const tasks = cat?.tasks || [];\r\n        const historyDigest = history.map((h) => [\r\n            getMondayStr(h?.date) || 'nodate',\r\n            Number(h?.score ?? 0),\r\n            Number(h?.correct ?? 0),\r\n            Number(h?.total ?? 0),\r\n            Array.isArray(h?.topics) ? h.topics.length : 0,\r\n            h?.taskId || ''\r\n        ].join(':')).join('|');\r\n        return [\r\n            cat?.id,\r\n            cat?.name || '',\r\n            tasks.length,\r\n            tasks.map((t) => `${t?.id || ''}:${t?.text || ''}`).join(','),\r\n            historyDigest\r\n        ].join('|');\r\n    }).join('||'), [categories]);\r\n\r\n    const { chartData, activeKeys, rankedKeys } = useMemo(() => {\r\n        let itemsMap = {};\r\n\r\n        if (!showOnlyFocus || !focusSubjectId) {\r\n            categories.forEach(cat => {\r\n                if (!cat?.id) return;\r\n                const fullName = String(cat.name || 'MatтФЬ┬оria').replace(/Direito /gi, 'D. ');\r\n                const safeName = shortenLabel(fullName, 18);\r\n                const safeColor = typeof cat.color === 'string' ? cat.color : '#3b82f6';\r\n                itemsMap[cat.id] = { name: safeName, fullName: fullName, color: safeColor };\r\n            });\r\n        } else {\r\n            const cat = categories.find(c => c.id === focusSubjectId);\r\n            if (cat) {\r\n                (cat.tasks || []).forEach(task => {\r\n                    const tName = String(task?.text || '').trim();\r\n                    if (!tName) return;\r\n                    itemsMap[tName.toLowerCase()] = { name: shortenLabel(tName, 18), color: cat.color || '#3b82f6', fullName: tName };\r\n                });\r\n\r\n                (cat.simuladoStats?.history || []).forEach(h => {\r\n                    if (h.topics && Array.isArray(h.topics)) {\r\n                        h.topics.forEach(t => {\r\n                            const tName = String(t.name || '').trim();\r\n                            if (!tName) return;\r\n                            if (!itemsMap[tName.toLowerCase()]) {\r\n                                itemsMap[tName.toLowerCase()] = { name: shortenLabel(tName, 18), color: cat.color || '#3b82f6', fullName: tName };\r\n                            }\r\n                        });\r\n                    } else if (h.taskId) {\r\n                        const tName = cat.tasks?.find(task => task.id === h.taskId)?.text || 'Assunto';\r\n                        if (!itemsMap[tName.toLowerCase()]) {\r\n                            itemsMap[tName.toLowerCase()] = { name: shortenLabel(tName, 18), color: cat.color || '#3b82f6', fullName: tName };\r\n                        }\r\n                    }\r\n                });\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        const validIds = Object.keys(itemsMap);\r\n        if (validIds.length === 0) return { chartData: [], activeKeys: {} };\r\n\r\n        const safeMinScore = Number.isFinite(Number(minScore)) ? Number(minScore) : 0;\r\n        const safeMaxScore = Number.isFinite(Number(maxScore)) ? Number(maxScore) : 100;\r\n        const lowerBound = Math.min(safeMinScore, safeMaxScore);\r\n        const upperBound = Math.max(safeMinScore, safeMaxScore);\r\n        const scoreRange = Math.max(1e-9, upperBound - lowerBound);\r\n        const toRatio = (score) => (Math.max(lowerBound, Math.min(upperBound, Number(score) || lowerBound)) - lowerBound) / scoreRange;\r\n        const fromRatio = (ratio) => lowerBound + (Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(ratio) || 0)) * scoreRange);\r\n        const weeksTemp = {};\r\n\r\n        const processHistory = (historyArray, itemId) => {\r\n            if (!Array.isArray(historyArray) || !itemId) return;\r\n            historyArray.forEach(h => {\r\n                const weekStr = getMondayStr(h.date);\r\n                if (!weekStr) return;\r\n\r\n                if (!weeksTemp[weekStr]) weeksTemp[weekStr] = { week: weekStr };\r\n                if (!weeksTemp[weekStr][itemId]) weeksTemp[weekStr][itemId] = { correct: 0, total: 0 };\r\n\r\n                let totalQ = Number(h.total) || 0;\r\n                const score = getSafeScore(h, upperBound);\r\n\r\n                if (totalQ === 0 && h.score != null) {\r\n                    totalQ = getSyntheticTotal(maxScore);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                weeksTemp[weekStr][itemId].total += totalQ;\r\n                weeksTemp[weekStr][itemId].correct += toRatio(score) * totalQ;\r\n            });\r\n        };\r\n\r\n        if (!showOnlyFocus || !focusSubjectId) {\r\n            categories.forEach(cat => {\r\n                processHistory(cat.simuladoStats?.history, cat.id);\r\n            });\r\n        } else {\r\n            const cat = categories.find(c => c.id === focusSubjectId);\r\n            if (cat) {\r\n                (cat.simuladoStats?.history || []).forEach(h => {\r\n                    if (h.topics && Array.isArray(h.topics)) {\r\n                        h.topics.forEach(t => {\r\n                            const tId = String(t.name || '').toLowerCase().trim();\r\n                            const weekStr = getMondayStr(h.date);\r\n                            if (!weekStr) return;\r\n                            if (!weeksTemp[weekStr]) weeksTemp[weekStr] = { week: weekStr };\r\n                            if (!weeksTemp[weekStr][tId]) weeksTemp[weekStr][tId] = { correct: 0, total: 0 };\r\n\r\n                            let totalQ = Number(t.total) || 0;\r\n                            const topicScore = getSafeScore(t, upperBound);\r\n                            if (totalQ === 0 && t.score != null) {\r\n                                totalQ = getSyntheticTotal(maxScore);\r\n                            }\r\n                            weeksTemp[weekStr][tId].total += totalQ;\r\n                            weeksTemp[weekStr][tId].correct += toRatio(topicScore) * totalQ;\r\n                        });\r\n                    } else if (h.taskId) {\r\n                        const tId = String(cat.tasks?.find(task => task.id === h.taskId)?.text || 'Assunto').toLowerCase().trim();\r\n                        processHistory([h], tId);\r\n                    }\r\n                });\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        const sortedWeeks = Object.values(weeksTemp).sort((a, b) => a.week.localeCompare(b.week));\r\n        if (sortedWeeks.length === 0) return { chartData: [], activeKeys: {}, rankedKeys: [] };\r\n\r\n        const memoryByItem = {}; \r\n\r\n        const finalData = sortedWeeks.map(weekObj => {\r\n            const dataPoint = {\r\n                week: weekObj.week,\r\n                displayDate: formatWeek(weekObj.week)\r\n            };\r\n\r\n            validIds.forEach(id => {\r\n                const currentData = weekObj[id];\r\n\r\n                if (currentData && currentData.total > 0) {\r\n                    const ratio = currentData.correct / currentData.total;\r\n                    const currentScore = fromRatio(ratio);\r\n                    const currentPct = Number(Math.max(lowerBound, Math.min(upperBound, currentScore)).toFixed(2));\r\n                    dataPoint[id] = currentPct;\r\n\r\n                    if (memoryByItem[id] !== undefined) {\r\n                        const prevPct = memoryByItem[id].pct;\r\n                        const delta = Number((currentPct - prevPct).toFixed(2));\r\n\r\n                        dataPoint[`delta_${id}`] = delta;\r\n                        dataPoint[`deltaColor_${id}`] = delta > 0 ? '#10b981' : delta < 0 ? '#ef4444' : '#94a3b8';\r\n\r\n                        dataPoint[`meta_${id}`] = {\r\n                            currTot: currentData.total,\r\n                            currPct: currentPct,\r\n                            prevPct: prevPct,\r\n                            prevTot: memoryByItem[id].total\r\n                        };\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        dataPoint[`delta_${id}`] = null;\r\n                        dataPoint[`deltaColor_${id}`] = '#94a3b8';\r\n                        dataPoint[`meta_${id}`] = { currTot: currentData.total, currPct: currentPct, prevPct: null, prevTot: 0 };\r\n                    }\r\n\r\n                    memoryByItem[id] = { pct: currentPct, total: currentData.total };\r\n                } else {\r\n                    dataPoint[id] = null;\r\n                    dataPoint[`delta_${id}`] = null;\r\n                    dataPoint[`deltaColor_${id}`] = '#94a3b8';\r\n                }\r\n            });\r\n\r\n            return dataPoint;\r\n        });\r\n\r\n        const volumeTracker = {};\r\n        validIds.forEach(id => volumeTracker[id] = 0);\r\n        finalData.forEach(week => {\r\n            validIds.forEach(id => {\r\n                const meta = week[`meta_${id}`];\r\n                if (meta && Number.isFinite(Number(meta.currTot))) volumeTracker[id] += Number(meta.currTot);\r\n            });\r\n        });\r\n        const rankedKeys = [...validIds].sort((a, b) => volumeTracker[b] - volumeTracker[a]);\r\n\r\n        return { chartData: finalData, activeKeys: itemsMap, rankedKeys };\r\n    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\r\n    }, [categories, showOnlyFocus, focusSubjectId, maxScore, minScore, categoriesSignature]);\r\n\r\n    const keys = Object.keys(activeKeys);\r\n\r\n    const hiddenKeys = useMemo(() => {\r\n        const result = {};\r\n        rankedKeys?.forEach((key, idx) => {\r\n            const defaultHide = showOnlyFocus ? false : idx >= 6; \r\n            if (userToggles[key] !== undefined) {\r\n                result[key] = userToggles[key]; \r\n            } else {\r\n                result[key] = defaultHide;\r\n            }\r\n        });\r\n        return result;\r\n    }, [rankedKeys, userToggles, showOnlyFocus]);\r\n\r\n    const topRegressions = useMemo(() => computeTopRegressions({ viewMode, chartData, keys, activeKeys, hiddenKeys }), [viewMode, chartData, keys, activeKeys, hiddenKeys]);\r\n    const trendKpi = useMemo(() => computeTrendKpi({ chartData, keys, hiddenKeys }), [chartData, keys, hiddenKeys]);\r\n\r\n    const handleLegendClick = useCallback((e) => {\r\n        const dataKey = e?.dataKey;\r\n        if (!dataKey) return;\r\n        const keyID = String(dataKey).replace('delta_', '');\r\n        setUserToggles(prev => ({\r\n            ...prev,\r\n            [keyID]: !hiddenKeys[keyID] \r\n        }));\r\n    }, [hiddenKeys]);\r\n\r\n    const handleLegendHover = useCallback((e) => {\r\n        if (e && e.dataKey) setHoveredLine(String(e.dataKey).replace('delta_', ''));\r\n    }, []);\r\n\r\n    const handleLegendLeave = useCallback(() => {\r\n        setHoveredLine(null);\r\n    }, []);\r\n\r\n    const renderLegendText = useCallback((value, entry) => {\r\n        const keyID = String(entry.dataKey || '').replace('delta_', '');\r\n        const isHidden = hiddenKeys[keyID];\r\n        return (\r\n            <span className={`text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest transition-opacity cursor-pointer ${isHidden ? 'opacity-20' : 'opacity-100'}`}>\r\n                {String(value || '').replace(' (Var.)', '')}\r\n            </span>\r\n        );\r\n    }, [hiddenKeys]);\r\n\r\n    if (chartData.length < 2) {\r\n        return (\r\n            <div className=\"h-[300px] flex flex-col items-center justify-center bg-slate-900/40 rounded-none border border-slate-800 p-6\">\r\n                <HelpCircle size={40} className=\"text-slate-600 mb-3\" />\r\n                <p className=\"text-slate-400 text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-center\">Dados Insuficientes</p>\r\n                <p className=\"text-slate-500 text-[10px] mt-2 text-center max-w-[250px]\">\r\n                    Registre pelo menos 2 semanas de simulados para visualizar a curva de evoluтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o e a variaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o de deltas.\r\n                </p>\r\n            </div>\r\n        );\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return (\r\n        <div className=\"w-full pt-4 animate-fade-in relative flex flex-col\">\r\n            <div className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-start sm:items-center justify-between mb-6 px-2 gap-4 shrink-0\">\r\n                <div>\r\n                    <h4 className=\"text-[10px] font-black text-indigo-400 uppercase tracking-[0.2em]\">Raio-X Temporal AvanтФЬ┬║ado</h4>\r\n                    <h3 className=\"text-lg font-black text-white uppercase tracking-tight\">\r\n                        {showOnlyFocus ? 'Semanas por Assunto' : 'Semanas por MatтФЬ┬оria'}\r\n                    </h3>\r\n                    {trendKpi && (\r\n                        <p className=\"text-[10px] mt-1 text-slate-400 font-mono\">\r\n                            TendтФЬ┬мncia: <span className={trendKpi.delta >= 0 ? 'text-emerald-300' : 'text-rose-300'}>{trendKpi.delta >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{formatValue(trendKpi.delta)}{unit}</span> \r\n                            {' '}({trendKpi.previousN} sem. ├Ф├е├Ж {trendKpi.recentN} sem.)\r\n                        </p>\r\n                    )}\r\n                </div>\r\n\r\n                <div className=\"flex items-center bg-slate-900/60 border border-slate-800 rounded-none p-1\">\r\n                    <button\r\n                        onClick={() => setViewMode('performance')}\r\n                        aria-label=\"Alternar para visтФЬ├║o de desempenho semanal\"\r\n                        aria-pressed={viewMode === 'performance'}\r\n                        className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-none text-[10px] font-bold uppercase transition-all ${viewMode === 'performance' ? 'bg-indigo-600/20 text-indigo-400' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300'}`}\r\n                    >\r\n                        <Zap size={14} /> Desempenho (7 dias)\r\n                    </button>\r\n                    <button\r\n                        onClick={() => setViewMode('evolution')}\r\n                        aria-label=\"Alternar para visтФЬ├║o de evoluтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o semanal\"\r\n                        aria-pressed={viewMode === 'evolution'}\r\n                        className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-none text-[10px] font-bold uppercase transition-all ${viewMode === 'evolution' ? 'bg-indigo-600/20 text-indigo-400' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300'}`}\r\n                    >\r\n                        <TrendingUp size={14} /> EvoluтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o\r\n                    </button>\r\n                    <button\r\n                        onClick={() => setViewMode('variation')}\r\n                        aria-label=\"Alternar para visтФЬ├║o de variaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o semanal\"\r\n                        aria-pressed={viewMode === 'variation'}\r\n                        className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-none text-[10px] font-bold uppercase transition-all ${viewMode === 'variation' ? 'bg-indigo-600/20 text-indigo-400' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300'}`}\r\n                    >\r\n                        <BarChart3 size={14} /> Delta\r\n                    </button>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n\r\n            <div className=\"h-[380px] w-full mt-2 relative\">\r\n                {viewMode === 'performance' ? (\r\n                    <WeeklyPerformanceChart\r\n                        categories={categories}\r\n                        studyLogs={studyLogs}\r\n                        showOnlyFocus={showOnlyFocus}\r\n                        focusSubjectId={focusSubjectId}\r\n                        maxScore={maxScore}\r\n                        unit={unit}\r\n                    />\r\n                ) : (\r\n                    <ResponsiveContainer width=\"100%\" height=\"100%\" minHeight={320}>\r\n                        {viewMode === 'evolution' ? (\r\n                            <LineChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 10, right: 10, left: 8, bottom: 0 }}>\r\n                                <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray=\"3 3\" stroke=\"#ffffff0a\" vertical={false} />\r\n\r\n                                <XAxis dataKey=\"displayDate\" stroke=\"#64748b\" fontSize={10} tickLine={false} axisLine={false} dy={10} minTickGap={15} />\r\n                                <YAxis domain={[minScore, maxScore]} stroke=\"#64748b\" fontSize={10} tickLine={false} axisLine={false} allowDataOverflow={true} tickFormatter={(v) => `${formatValue(v)}${unit}`} />\r\n                                <Tooltip offset={200} content={<WeeklyTooltip hiddenKeys={hiddenKeys} unit={unit} />} cursor={{ stroke: '#ffffff22', strokeWidth: 1, strokeDasharray: '4 4' }} />\r\n                                <Legend verticalAlign=\"bottom\" height={40} iconType=\"circle\" formatter={renderLegendText} onClick={handleLegendClick} onMouseEnter={handleLegendHover} onMouseLeave={handleLegendLeave} wrapperStyle={{ paddingTop: '20px' }} />\r\n\r\n                                {keys.map(key => {\r\n                                    const isHovered = hoveredLine === key;\r\n                                    const isOtherHovered = hoveredLine && hoveredLine !== key;\r\n                                    \r\n                                    return (\r\n                                        <Line\r\n                                            key={key}\r\n                                            type=\"monotoneX\"\r\n                                            dataKey={key}\r\n                                            name={activeKeys[key].name}\r\n                                            stroke={activeKeys[key].color}\r\n                                            strokeWidth={isHovered ? 3.5 : (isOtherHovered ? 1.5 : 2)}\r\n                                            strokeOpacity={isOtherHovered ? 0.4 : 1}\r\n                                            dot={{ r: 3, strokeWidth: 1.5, stroke: activeKeys[key].color, fill: '#0f172a', strokeOpacity: isOtherHovered ? 0.4 : 1, fillOpacity: isOtherHovered ? 0.4 : 1 }}\r\n                                            activeDot={{ r: 5, strokeWidth: 2, stroke: '#ffffff', fill: activeKeys[key].color, className: 'shadow-lg', opacity: isOtherHovered ? 0.4 : 1 }}\r\n                                            hide={hiddenKeys[key]}\r\n                                            isAnimationActive={true}\r\n                                            connectNulls={true}\r\n                                            style={{ transition: 'all 0.3s ease' }}\r\n                                        />\r\n                                    );\r\n                                })}\r\n\r\n                                {chartData.length > 8 && (\r\n                                    <Brush\r\n                                        dataKey=\"week\"\r\n                                        height={18}\r\n                                        stroke=\"#ffffff11\"\r\n                                        fill=\"#0f172a\"\r\n                                        tickFormatter={formatWeek}\r\n                                        className=\"text-[8px]\"\r\n                                        travellerWidth={8}\r\n                                    />\r\n                                )}\r\n                            </LineChart>\r\n                        ) : (\r\n                            <BarChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 10, right: 10, left: 8, bottom: 0 }}>\r\n                                <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray=\"3 3\" stroke=\"#ffffff0a\" vertical={false} />\r\n\r\n                                <XAxis dataKey=\"displayDate\" stroke=\"#64748b\" fontSize={10} tickLine={false} axisLine={false} dy={10} minTickGap={15} />\r\n                                {/* ┬н╞Т├Д┬╗ FIX: Uso do formatValue e correcтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o lтФЬтФВgica para o sinal de mais (+) e o Zero perfeito */}\r\n                                <YAxis \r\n                                    stroke=\"#64748b\" \r\n                                    fontSize={10} \r\n                                    tickLine={false} \r\n                                    axisLine={false} \r\n                                    tickFormatter={(v) => {\r\n                                        if (v === 0) return `0${unit}`;\r\n                                        return `${v > 0 ? '+' : ''}${formatValue(v)}${unit}`;\r\n                                    }} \r\n                                />\r\n                                <Legend verticalAlign=\"bottom\" height={40} iconType=\"square\" formatter={renderLegendText} onClick={handleLegendClick} onMouseEnter={handleLegendHover} onMouseLeave={handleLegendLeave} wrapperStyle={{ paddingTop: '20px' }} />\r\n                                <ReferenceLine y={0} stroke=\"#ffffff22\" />\r\n\r\n                                {chartData.length > 8 && (\r\n                                    <Brush\r\n                                        dataKey=\"week\"\r\n                                        height={18}\r\n                                        stroke=\"#ffffff11\"\r\n                                        fill=\"#0f172a\"\r\n                                        tickFormatter={formatWeek}\r\n                                        className=\"text-[8px]\"\r\n                                        travellerWidth={8}\r\n                                    />\r\n                                )}\r\n\r\n                                {keys.map(key => {\r\n                                    const isHovered = hoveredLine === key;\r\n                                    const isOtherHovered = hoveredLine && hoveredLine !== key;\r\n\r\n                                    return (\r\n                                        <Bar\r\n                                            key={`delta_${key}`}\r\n                                            dataKey={`delta_${key}`}\r\n                                            name={`${activeKeys[key].name} (Var.)`}\r\n                                            fill={activeKeys[key].color}\r\n                                            radius={[0, 0, 0, 0]}\r\n                                            hide={hiddenKeys[key]}\r\n                                            fillOpacity={isOtherHovered ? 0.4 : 1}\r\n                                            style={{ transition: 'all 0.3s ease' }}\r\n                                        >\r\n                                            {chartData.map((entry, index) => {\r\n                                                const barColor = entry[`deltaColor_${key}`] || '#94a3b8';\r\n                                                return <Cell key={`cell-${index}`} fill={barColor} fillOpacity={isOtherHovered ? 0.4 : 0.85} />;\r\n                                            })}\r\n                                        </Bar>\r\n                                    );\r\n                                })}\r\n                            </BarChart>\r\n                        )}\r\n                    </ResponsiveContainer>\r\n                )}\r\n            </div>\r\n\r\n            {viewMode === 'variation' && (\r\n                <div className=\"mt-3 rounded-none border border-rose-900/40 bg-rose-950/20 p-3\">\r\n                    <p className=\"text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-rose-300 mb-2\">\r\n                        Top RegressтФЬ├Бes {topRegressions[0]?.week ? `тФм├А Semana ${topRegressions[0].week}` : ''}\r\n                    </p>\r\n                    {topRegressions.length > 0 ? (\r\n                        <div className=\"grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-2\">\r\n                            {topRegressions.map(item => (\r\n                                <div key={item.key} className=\"rounded-none bg-black/30 border border-white/5 px-2 py-1.5 text-[10px] flex items-center justify-between\">\r\n                                    <span className=\"truncate\" style={{ color: item.color }} title={item.fullName}>{item.name}</span>\r\n                                    <span className=\"font-mono font-black   <script>
    window.addEventListener('error', (event) => {
      const loaderText = document.querySelector('.loader-text');

      if (!loaderText) return;

      loaderText.textContent = 'Erro de carregamento: ' + event.message;
      loaderText.style.color = '#f87171';
      loaderText.style.animation = 'none';
    });

    const BUILD_VERSION = "2026-07-21-FIX"; // ideal: injetar via build/env
    const buildVersion = typeof BUILD_VERSION !== 'undefined' ? BUILD_VERSION : (window.__BUILD_VERSION__ || 'dev');
    console.log("[Build] Vers├Г┬гo:", buildVersion);

    setTimeout(() => {
      const loaderText = document.querySelector('.loader-text');
      if (!loaderText) return;

      const currentText = loaderText.textContent || "";
      if (!currentText.includes("Carregando")) return;

      loaderText.textContent = "";

      const title = document.createElement("div");
      title.textContent = "Carregamento lento detectado...";

      const version = document.createElement("small");
      version.style.opacity = "0.5";
      version.textContent = `Vers├Г┬гo: ${buildVersion} | Verifique o painel VITE_.`;

      const btn = document.createElement("button");
      btn.textContent = "Limpar dados e reiniciar";
      btn.style.marginTop = "20px";
      btn.style.background = "rgba(248, 113, 113, 0.2)";
      btn.style.border = "1px solid #f87171";
      btn.style.color = "#f87171";
      btn.style.padding = "8px 16px";
      btn.style.borderRadius = "8px";
      btn.style.cursor = "pointer";
      btn.style.fontSize = "12px";

      async function clearAllLocalData() {
        try {
          localStorage.clear();
          sessionStorage.clear();

          if ('indexedDB' in window && typeof indexedDB.databases === 'function') {
            const dbs = await indexedDB.databases();

            if (Array.isArray(dbs)) {
              dbs.forEach(db => {
                if (db.name) indexedDB.deleteDatabase(db.name);
              });
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Erro ao limpar dados locais:', error);
        } finally {
          location.reload();
        }
      }

      btn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
        const ok = window.confirm(
          "Isso apagar├Г┬б os dados locais deste navegador. Deseja continuar?"
        );

        if (ok) {
          await clearAllLocalData();
        }
      });

      loaderText.appendChild(title);
      loaderText.appendChild(document.createElement("br"));
      loaderText.appendChild(version);
      loaderText.appendChild(document.createElement("br"));
      loaderText.appendChild(btn);
    }, 8000);
  </script>

Math.round((correct / total) * 100) : 0,\n        total,\n        correct,\n        type: 'ai-simulado',\n        subject: materia,\n        categoryId,\n        taskId,\n        validated: true,\n      };\n\n      const existingSims = Array.isArray(prev.simulados) ? prev.simulados : [];\n      // Apenas remove eventos AI do mesmo dia (nтФЬ├║o apaga eventos do analyzer)\n      const simsWithoutToday = existingSims.filter(s => !(s.date === todayKey && (s.type === 'ai-simulado' || s.source === 'ai')));\n      const updatedSims = [...simsWithoutToday, newSimEvent].slice(-100);\n\n      // 3. Atualiza stats da categoria ├Ф├З├╢ preferindo match por ID exato (mais confiтФЬ├нvel)\n      const newCategories = (prev.categories || []).map(cat => {\n        const idMatch = categoryId && cat.id === categoryId;\n        const nameMatch = !categoryId && normalize(cat.name) === normalize(materia);\n        if (idMatch || nameMatch) {\n          const catMaxScore = Number(cat.maxScore) || Number(prev.maxScore) || 100;\n          let history = Array.isArray(cat.simuladoStats?.history) ? [...cat.simuladoStats.history] : [];\n\n          // Melhorias lтФЬтФВgicas: \n          // - NтФЬ├║o apagar todo o dia se jтФЬ├н existir entrada (permite mтФЬтХСltiplos tтФЬтФВpicos AI no mesmo dia)\n          // - Encontrar ou criar entrada de hoje e fazer merge do tтФЬтФВpico\n          const todayIdx = history.findIndex(h => h.date === todayKey);\n\n          const newTopicEntry = { name: assunto, correct, total, taskId };\n\n          if (todayIdx !== -1) {\n            // Merge no entry de hoje existente\n            const existing = { ...history[todayIdx] };\n            const existingTopics = Array.isArray(existing.topics) ? existing.topics.filter(t => {\n              if (taskId && t.taskId) return t.taskId !== taskId;\n              // fallback for legacy without taskId\n              return normalize(t.name) !== normalize(assunto);\n            }) : [];\n            existingTopics.push(newTopicEntry);\n\n            // Recalcular totais do dia\n            const dayTotal = existingTopics.reduce((s, t) => s + (t.total || 0), 0);\n            const dayCorrect = existingTopics.reduce((s, t) => s + (t.correct || 0), 0);\n\n            history[todayIdx] = {\n              ...existing,\n              correct: dayCorrect,\n              total: dayTotal,\n              score: dayTotal > 0 ? Math.min(catMaxScore, (dayCorrect / dayTotal) * catMaxScore) : 0,\n              topics: existingTopics,\n              // MantтФЬ┬оm difficulty do тФЬтХСltimo ou podemos mтФЬ┬оdia\n            };\n          } else {\n            history.push({\n              date: todayKey,\n              correct,\n              total,\n              score: total > 0 ? Math.min(catMaxScore, (correct / total) * catMaxScore) : 0,\n              difficulty: formData.dificuldade === 'facil' ? 0.7 : formData.dificuldade === 'medio' ? 1.0 : formData.dificuldade === 'dificil' ? 1.3 : 1.6,\n              topics: [newTopicEntry],\n            });\n          }\n\n          // Ordenar por data (тФЬтХСltimos primeiro ou como esperado)\n          history = history.sort((a, b) => (a.date > b.date ? 1 : -1)).slice(-50);\n\n          const statsResult = computeCategoryStats(history, cat.weight || 1, 60, catMaxScore);\n\n          return {\n            ...cat,\n            simuladoStats: {\n              ...(cat.simuladoStats || {}),\n              history: history,\n              average: statsResult ? Number((statsResult.mean || 0).toFixed(2)) : 0,\n              trend: statsResult?.trend || 'stable',\n              lastAttempt: total > 0 ? (correct / total) * catMaxScore : 0,\n              level: statsResult?.level || 'BAIXO',\n            },\n          };\n        }\n        return cat;\n      });\n\n      return {\n        ...prev,\n        simuladoRows: updatedRows,\n        simulados: updatedSims,\n        categories: newCategories,\n        lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString(),\n      };\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleFinish = useCallback(async () => {\n    // Use refs for the case when called from timer (avoids stale state)\n    const qList = latestQuestionsRef.current.length > 0 ? latestQuestionsRef.current : questions;\n    const ansMap = Object.keys(latestAnswersRef.current).length > 0 ? latestAnswersRef.current : answers;\n    const f = latestFormRef.current;\n\n    if (qList.length === 0) return;\n\n    // Evita chamadas duplas (timer + clique) usando ref\n    if (isFinishingRef.current || step === 'finished') return;\n    isFinishingRef.current = true;\n\n    let correctCount = 0;\n    const answeredQuestions = [];\n\n    qList.forEach(q => {\n      const selected = ansMap[q.id];\n      const isCorrect = selected === q.alternativa_correta;\n      if (isCorrect) correctCount++;\n\n      answeredQuestions.push({\n        ...q,\n        selected,\n        isCorrect,\n      });\n    });\n\n    const total = qList.length;\n    const scorePercent = total > 0 ? Math.round((correctCount / total) * 100) : 0;\n\n    // === SALVA NO SISTEMA (mesma infraestrutura dos simulados) ===\n    await saveAIResultsToSystem(f, correctCount, total, answeredQuestions);\n\n    setResults({\n      correct: correctCount,\n      total,\n      scorePercent,\n      questions: answeredQuestions,\n    });\n    setStep('finished');\n    setTimerActive(false);\n    localStorage.removeItem(AI_SIM_STORAGE_KEY);\n    showToast(`Simulado finalizado! ${correctCount}/${total} acertos`, 'success');\n\n    // reset flag (though component will unmount the playing logic)\n    setTimeout(() => { isFinishingRef.current = false; }, 0);\n  }, [step]);  // step for the early guard; refs are stable\n\n  // Timer effect (declared after handleFinish to avoid TDZ in deps)\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let interval = null;\n    if (timerActive && timeLeft > 0 && step === 'playing') {\n      interval = setInterval(() => {\n        setTimeLeft((prev) => {\n          if (prev <= 1) {\n            handleFinish();\n            return 0;\n          }\n          return prev - 1;\n        });\n      }, 1000);\n    }\n    return () => clearInterval(interval);\n  }, [timerActive, timeLeft, step, handleFinish]);\n\n  const resetAll = () => {\n    isFinishingRef.current = false;\n    setStep('setup');\n    setQuestions([]);\n    setAnswers({});\n    setCurrentIndex(0);\n    setResults(null);\n    setTimeLeft(45 * 60);\n    setTimerActive(false);\n    setShowReview(false);\n    localStorage.removeItem(AI_SIM_STORAGE_KEY);\n    // mantтФЬ┬оm o form para nova geraтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o rтФЬ├нpida\n  };\n\n  const retrySameQuestions = () => {\n    isFinishingRef.current = false;\n    setAnswers({});\n    setCurrentIndex(0);\n    setResults(null);\n    setTimeLeft(45 * 60);\n    setTimerActive(true);\n    setShowReview(false);\n    setStep('playing');\n    showToast('QuestтФЬ├Бes reiniciadas. Boa sorte!', 'info');\n  };\n\n  // Keyboard shortcuts (placed after handler defs)\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (step !== 'playing' || !currentQuestion) return;\n    const handleKeyDown = (e) => {\n      const key = e.key.toUpperCase();\n      const curIdx = latestCurrentIndexRef.current;\n      const qLen = latestQuestionsRef.current.length || questions.length;\n      if (['A','B','C','D'].includes(key)) { e.preventDefault(); selectAnswer(key); }\n      else if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft') { e.preventDefault(); goTo(curIdx - 1); }\n      else if (e.key === 'ArrowRight' || e.key === 'Enter') {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        if (curIdx < qLen - 1) goTo(curIdx + 1); else handleFinish();\n      } else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'escape') {\n        e.preventDefault(); setTimerActive(false); setStep('setup');\n      }\n    };\n    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);\n    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);\n  }, [step, currentQuestion, handleFinish, questions.length]);\n\n  // ==================== RENDER ====================\n\n  if (step === 'setup') {\n    const hasApiKey = !!(import.meta.env.VITE_OPENAI_API_KEY || import.meta.env.VITE_GEMINI_API_KEY);\n    const isReadyToGenerate = form.categoryId && form.taskId && hasApiKey;\n\n    return (\n      <motion.div \n        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}\n        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\n        exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}\n        className=\"max-w-2xl mx-auto\"\n      >\n        {/* ├Ф├▓├Й├Ф├▓├Й├Ф├▓├Й HERO HEADER ├Ф├▓├Й├Ф├▓├Й├Ф├▓├Й */}\n        <div className=\"relative mb-8 overflow-hidden rounded-[28px] border border-white/[0.06]\" style={{ background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(49,46,129,0.4) 0%, rgba(15,23,42,0.9) 50%, rgba(88,28,135,0.3) 100%)' }}>\n          {/* Animated glow orbs */}\n          <div className=\"absolute -left-20 -top-20 w-60 h-60 bg-indigo-500/20 rounded-full blur-[80px] animate-pulse\" />\n          <div className=\"absolute -right-16 -bottom-16 w-48 h-48 bg-purple-500/15 rounded-full blur-[60px]\" style={{ animationDelay: '1s' }} />\n          <div className=\"absolute left-1/2 top-0 w-px h-full bg-gradient-to-b from-indigo-400/20 via-transparent to-purple-400/20\" />\n          \n          <div className=\"relative px-8 py-10 sm:px-10\">\n            <div className=\"flex items-start gap-5\">\n              {/* Animated icon */}\n              <motion.div \n                animate={{ rotate: [0, 5, -5, 0] }}\n                transition={{ repeat: Infinity, duration: 4, ease: \"easeInOut\" }}\n                className=\"shrink-0 p-4 rounded-2xl border border-indigo-400/30 shadow-[0_0_30px_rgba(99,102,241,0.2)]\"\n                style={{ background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(99,102,241,0.25), rgba(147,51,234,0.25))' }}\n              >\n                <Brain size={36} className=\"text-indigo-300\" />\n              </motion.div>\n              <div className=\"flex-1 min-w-0\">\n                <div className=\"flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2.5 mb-2\">\n                  <h2 className=\"text-[28px] sm:text-3xl font-black tracking-[-1px] text-white\">Simulado IA</h2>\n                  <span className=\"inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-[9px] px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full font-black tracking-[2px] uppercase bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-400 border border-emerald-500/25\">\n                    <Sparkles size={10} /> OFICIAL\n                  </span>\n                </div>\n                <p <BarChart3 size={12} className=\"text-purple-400\" />\n                <span>Atualiza Dashboard</span>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2 text-xs VINCULADO ├Ф┬г├┤\n                  </div>\n                )}\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"space-y-5\">\n                {/* MatтФЬ┬оria + Assunto - Visual melhorado e         {/* MatтФЬ┬оria */}\n                    <div className=\"group\">\n                      <label className=\"flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-extrabold tracking-[1.5px] text-indigo-300/90 />\n                      </div>\n                      {categories.length === 0 && (\n                        <div className=\"mt-2 text-[11px] bg-rose-500/10 border border-rose-500/20 text-rose-400            </div>\n\n                    {/* Assunto */}\n                    <div className=\"group\">\n                      <label className=\"flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-extrabold                  <select\n                          value={form.taskId}\n                          onChange={(e) => handleTaskSelect(e.target.value)}\n                          disabled={!form.categoryId || availableTasks.length === 0}\n                          className=\"w-full bg-slate-950/80 border border-white/10 focus:border-indigo-400/70 focus:bg-slate-900                        >\n                          <option value=\"\">Selecione o assunto...</option>\n                          {[...availableTasks].sort((a,b) => </div>\n\n                  {/* Resumo da seleтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o - Feedback visual forte */}\n                  {(form.categoryId || form.taskId) && (\n                    <div className=\"mt-4 pt-4 border-t text-indigo-400/60\">├Ф├ЗтХС</span>}\n                        {form.assunto || ''}\n                      </div>\n                      {form.categoryId && form.taskId && (\n                        <div className=\"text-[10px] px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-indigo-500/10 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/20 font-bold\">PRONTO</div>\n                      )}\n                    </div>\n                  )}\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            {/* Separator */}\n            <div className=\"h-px bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/[0.08]         <label className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[11px] font-bold text-slate-400 mb-3 tracking-[1px] uppercase\">\n                  <Target size={12} /> Dificuldade\n                </label>\n                <div className=\"flex gap-1.5\">\n                  {DIFFICULTIES.map(d => (\n                    <button\n                      key={d.value}\n                      type=\"button\"\n                      onClick={() => handleInputChange('dificuldade', d.value)}\n                      className={`flex-1 py-2.5 text-[12px] font-bold rounded-xl border transition-all { scale: 1.01 } : {}}\n              whileTap={isReadyToGenerate && !isLoading ? { scale: 0.985 } : {}}\n              className=\"group relative mt-8 w-full py-5 rounded-2xl font-black text-[15px] tracking-[2px] transition-all duration-300 flex items-center justify-center gap-3 overflow-hidden disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed\"\n              style={{ \n                background: isReadyToGenerate && !isLoading \n                  ? (\n                  <>\n                    <div className=\"w-5 h-5 border-2 border-white/30 border-t-white rounded-full animate-spin\" />\n                    <span>SINTETIZANDO QUESTтФЬ├▓ES...</span>\n                  </>\n                ) : (\n                  <>\n                    <Brain size={22} className={isReadyToGenerate ? [];\r\n        historicalCutoffs = meanOrObj.historicalCutoffs ?? [];\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const safeDomain = sanitizeDomain(minScore, maxScore);\r\n    minScore = safeDomain.minScore;\r\n    maxScore = safeDomain.maxScore;\r\n\r\n    const safeMean = Number.isFinite(mean) ? mean : 0;\r\n    const hasExplicitDeterministicSD = Number.isFinite(sd) && sd <= 0;\r\n    let safeSD = Number.isFinite(sd) && sd > 0 ? sd : 0; \r\n\r\n    // FIX: Unificar a inferтФЬ┬мncia do SD nos dois caminhos\r\n    if (bayesianCI) {\r\n        // SD SQUASH (Fix): Usar os limites NтФЬ├вO truncados para inferir o SD real.\r\n        // Se usarmos ciHigh truncado em 100, o SD serтФЬ├н subestimado para alunos de elite.\r\n        const high = bayesianCI.unclampedHigh !== undefined ? bayesianCI.unclampedHigh : bayesianCI.ciHigh;\r\n        const low = bayesianCI.unclampedLow !== undefined ? bayesianCI.unclampedLow : bayesianCI.ciLow;\r\n        \r\n        if (high !== undefined && low !== undefined) {\r\n            // CORREтФЬ├зтФЬ├вO: Usar o mesmo T-Multiplier dinтФЬ├│mico que gerou o CI, em vez da constante estтФЬ├нtica 3.92\r\n            const effectiveN = bayesianCI.n || Math.max(1, historyLength);\r\n            const tMultiplier = getConfidenceMultiplier(effectiveN, { allowFractional: true });\r\n            \r\n            let inferredSD = (high - low) / (tMultiplier * 2);\r\n            const distToBoundary = Math.min(safeMean - minScore, maxScore - safeMean);\r\n \r\n            // Se a mтФЬ┬оdia estiver muito prтФЬтФВxima do limite (0 ou 100), o intervalo de 95% \r\n            // fica comprimido. Inflamos o SD para refletir a incerteza real.\r\n            if (Number.isFinite(inferredSD) && inferredSD >= 1e-10) {\r\n                if (distToBoundary < inferredSD * 1.5) {\r\n                    const correctionFactor = 1 + (1 - distToBoundary / (inferredSD * 1.5));\r\n                    inferredSD *= Math.min(1.5, correctionFactor);\r\n                }\r\n            }\r\n            if (Number.isFinite(inferredSD) && inferredSD > 0) {\r\n                safeSD = inferredSD;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n    }\r\n \r\n    // O PULO DO GATO: Shrinkage Bayesiano para safeSD (Bug 1 Fix)\r\n    // Se temos um histтФЬтФВrico curto, nтФЬ├║o podemos confiar em SD=0.\r\n    if (!hasExplicitDeterministicSD && historyLength < 15) {\r\n        const floorVolatility = maxScore * 0.04;\r\n        const confidence = historyLength / 15;\r\n        safeSD = (safeSD * confidence) + (floorVolatility * (1 - confidence));\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // MATH-05/10 FIX: Use same effective target for empirical and analytic\r\n    // Clamp target to simulation domain\r\n    const effectiveTarget = Math.max(minScore, Math.min(maxScore, targetScore));\r\n\r\n    const safeSimulations = sanitizeSimulations(simulations);\r\n\r\n    if (safeSD < 1e-5) {\r\n        const prob = safeMean >= effectiveTarget ? 100 : 0;\r\n        return {\r\n            simulationCount: safeSimulations,\r\n            probability: prob,\r\n            analyticalProbability: prob,\r\n            recommendedProbability: prob,\r\n            probabilityPolicy: 'deterministic',\r\n            // FIX #2: Retornar valores com precisтФЬ├║o completa (formataтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o sтФЬтФВ na UI)\r\n            mean: safeMean,\r\n            sd: 0,\r\n            sdVisual: 0,\r\n            sdLeft: 0, \r\n            sdRight: 0, \r\n            ci95StatLow: safeMean,\r\n            ci95StatHigh: safeMean,\r\n            ci95Low: safeMean,\r\n            ci95High: safeMean,\r\n            ci95VisualLow: safeMean,\r\n            ci95VisualHigh: safeMean,\r\n            ci95VisualClamped: false,\r\n            currentMean: (currentMean ?? safeMean),\r\n            projectedMean: safeMean,\r\n            projectedSD: 0,\r\n            kdeData: [\r\n                // BUGFIX VISUAL: Adicionada a chave 'density' para evitar quebra do Recharts\r\n                safeMean > minScore ? { x: safeMean - 0.1, y: 0, density: 0 } : null,\r\n                { x: safeMean, y: 1, density: 1 },\r\n                safeMean < maxScore ? { x: safeMean + 0.1, y: 0, density: 0 } : null\r\n            ].filter(Boolean), \r\n            drift: 0,\r\n            volatility: 0,\r\n            minScore,\r\n            maxScore,\r\n            method: bayesianCI ? 'bayesian_static_hybrid' : 'deterministic'\r\n        };\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // SUBSTITUIтФЬ├зтФЬ├вO DA LтФЬ├┤GICA DE SEMENTE ANTIGA:\r\n    // Remover o hash fraco (Math.floor(safeMean * 10000)) que causava o layout shift.\r\n    const stableSeed = seed ?? generateStableSeed(historyLength, categoryName, targetScore);\r\n\r\n    const rng = mulberry32(stableSeed);\r\n    let success = 0;\r\n\r\n    let welfordMean = 0;\r\n    let welfordM2 = 0;\r\n    let welfordCount = 0;\r\n\r\n    // InstanciaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o local para garantir thread-safety e evitar data races\r\n    const allScores = new Float64Array(safeSimulations);\r\n\r\n    // CORREтФЬ├зтФЬ├вO MATEMтФЬ├╝TICA: CompensaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o Exata da MтФЬ┬оdia da Normal Truncada\r\n    // Substitui a heurтФЬ┬бstica de repulsтФЬ├║o exponencial pela fтФЬтФВrmula analтФЬ┬бtica exata:\r\n    // E[X] = тХмтХЭ + ┬д├втФм├А(┬д├е(тХмтЦТ) - ┬д├е(тХмтЦУ))/(тХм┬к(тХмтЦУ) - тХм┬к(тХмтЦТ))\r\n    // Isso garante que a mтФЬ┬оdia empтФЬ┬бrica das simulaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├Бes convirja para o valor correto\r\n    // em todos os cenтФЬ├нrios (bordas, centro, qualquer escala).\r\n    //\r\n    // Para o cтФЬ├нlculo ANALтФЬ├мTICO da probabilidade, usamos safeMean diretamente (sem\r\n    // compensaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o), pois a fтФЬтФВrmula da P(X ├Ф├л├С target) na Normal Truncada jтФЬ├н тФЬ┬о exata.\r\n    // A compensaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o de muParam sтФЬтФВ serve para a amostragem (onde precisamos deslocar\r\n    // тХмтХЭ para que as amostras tenham E[X] = safeMean apтФЬтФВs truncagem).\r\n    let muParam = safeMean;\r\n    \r\n    if (safeSD > 0) {\r\n        // Calcular a mтФЬ┬оdia real que a Normal Truncada produziria com тХмтХЭ = safeMean\r\n        const expectedTruncMean = truncatedNormalMean(safeMean, safeSD, minScore, maxScore);\r\n        // O viтФЬ┬оs introduzido pela truncagem\r\n        const truncationBias = expectedTruncMean - safeMean;\r\n        // Compensar: se a truncagem puxa a mтФЬ┬оdia para cima, desloco тХмтХЭ para baixo\r\n        muParam = safeMean - truncationBias;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // FEATURE 2: Preparar distribuiтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o de cortes histтФЬтФВricos se houver\r\n    let cutoffsMean = 0;\r\n    let cutoffsSD = 0;\r\n    const hasCutoffs = Array.isArray(historicalCutoffs) && historicalCutoffs.length > 0;\r\n    if (hasCutoffs) {\r\n        // BUG-8 FIX: Usar acumulador explтФЬ┬бcito com initial value 0 para evitar\r\n        // que o primeiro elemento (potencialmente string) seja usado como seed.\r\n        const numericCutoffs = historicalCutoffs.map(v => Number(v)).filter(Number.isFinite);\r\n        if (numericCutoffs.length > 0) {\r\n            cutoffsMean = kahanSum(numericCutoffs) / numericCutoffs.length;\r\n            if (numericCutoffs.length > 1) {\r\n                const devs = numericCutoffs.map(v => Math.pow(v - cutoffsMean, 2));\r\n                cutoffsSD = Math.sqrt( kahanSum(devs) / (numericCutoffs.length - 1) );\r\n            } else {\r\n                cutoffsSD = cutoffsMean * 0.05; // 5% default SD\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // FIX #3: Prepare Cholesky for correlated subject minCutoffs (when >1 subjects with minCutoff)\r\n    const cutoffSubjects = (subjects || []).filter(s => s && Number(s.minCutoff) > 0);\r\n    let subjectCholesky = null;\r\n    if (cutoffSubjects.length > 1) {\r\n      const stats = cutoffSubjects.map(s => ({ sd: Number(s.sd) || 1 }));\r\n      const adaptiveRhoContext = (meanOrObj?.simuladoRows || options?.simuladoRows) \r\n        ? { simuladoRows: meanOrObj?.simuladoRows || options?.simuladoRows, categoryNames: subjects.map(s => s.name || s) } \r\n        : null;\r\n      const cov = buildCovarianceMatrix(stats, null, INTER_SUBJECT_CORRELATION, adaptiveRhoContext);\r\n      const psdCov = ensurePositiveSemiDefinite(cov);\r\n      subjectCholesky = choleskyDecomposition(psdCov);\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    for (let i = 0; i < safeSimulations; i++) {\r\n        let currentTarget = effectiveTarget;\r\n        if (hasCutoffs) {\r\n            // Sorteio inteligente do cutoff usando a distribuiтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o dos cortes histтФЬтФВricos\r\n            currentTarget = sampleTruncatedNormal(cutoffsMean, cutoffsSD, minScore, maxScore, rng);\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        let score = sampleTruncatedNormal(muParam, safeSD, minScore, maxScore, rng);\r\n        \r\n        let passedMins = true;\r\n        if (cutoffSubjects.length > 0) {\r\n            if (subjectCholesky) {\r\n                // Generate independent standard normals, apply correlation via Cholesky\r\n                const zVec = cutoffSubjects.map(() => generateGaussian(rng));\r\n                const zCorr = applyCovariance(subjectCholesky, zVec);\r\n                for (let j = 0; j < cutoffSubjects.length; j++) {\r\n                    const s = cutoffSubjects[j];\r\n                    const sMin = Number.isFinite(s.minScore) ? s.minScore : minScore;\r\n                    const sMax = Number.isFinite(s.maxScore) ? s.maxScore : maxScore;\r\n                    const raw = Number(s.mean) + zCorr[j] * (Number(s.sd) || 1);\r\n                    const sScore = Math.max(sMin, Math.min(sMax, raw));\r\n                    if (sScore < Number(s.minCutoff)) {\r\n                        passedMins = false;\r\n                        break;\r\n                    }\r\n                }\r\n            } else {\r\n                // fallback: independent sampling (0 or 1 subject)\r\n                for (let j = 0; j < cutoffSubjects.length; j++) {\r\n                    const s = cutoffSubjects[j];\r\n                    const sMin = Number.isFinite(s.minScore) ? s.minScore : minScore;\r\n                    const sMax = Number.isFinite(s.maxScore) ? s.maxScore : maxScore;\r\n                    const sScore = sampleTruncatedNormal(s.mean, s.sd, sMin, sMax, rng);\r\n                    if (sScore < s.minCutoff) {\r\n                        passedMins = false;\r\n                        break;\r\n                    }\r\n                }\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n        \r\n        if (score >= currentTarget && passedMins) success++;\r\n        allScores[i] = score;\r\n\r\n        welfordCount++;\r\n        const delta = score - welfordMean;\r\n        welfordMean += delta / welfordCount;\r\n        welfordM2 += delta * (score - welfordMean);\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const projectedMean = welfordMean;\r\n    const projectedSD = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, welfordCount > 1 ? welfordM2 / (welfordCount - 1) : 0));\r\n\r\n    // MELHORIA-3: OrdenaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o тФЬтХСnica em vez de 5тФЬ├╣ quickSelect (que criava 5 cтФЬтФВpias de Float64Array).\r\n    // Para N=5000, isso reduz de ~125KB de alocaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├Бes para ~40KB (1 cтФЬтФВpia ordenada).\r\n    // A ordenaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o nativa de Float64Array usa radix sort no V8 (O(N)), tтФЬ├║o rтФЬ├нpida quanto quickSelect.\r\n    const sortedScores = new Float64Array(allScores);\r\n    sortedScores.sort();\r\n    \r\n    // Leitura usando funтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o de percentil interpolada para consistтФЬ┬мncia matemтФЬ├нtica no sistema\r\n    const statisticalCi95Low = getPercentile(sortedScores, 0.025, true);\r\n    const statisticalCi95High = getPercentile(sortedScores, 0.975, true);\r\n    const empMedian = getPercentile(sortedScores, 0.5, true);\r\n    const rawLeft = getPercentile(sortedScores, 0.16, true);\r\n    const rawRight = getPercentile(sortedScores, 0.84, true);\r\n\r\n    let rawLow = statisticalCi95Low;\r\n    let rawHigh = statisticalCi95High;\r\n\r\n    const empiricalProbability = (success / safeSimulations) * 100;\r\n    // SuavizaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o Bayesiana (Jeffreys prior) para reduzir ruтФЬ┬бdo em baixa amostra.\r\n    const posteriorAlpha = success + 0.5;\r\n    const posteriorBeta = (safeSimulations - success) + 0.5;\r\n    const bayesEmpiricalProbability = (posteriorAlpha / (posteriorAlpha + posteriorBeta)) * 100;\r\n    const displayMean = bayesianCI ? safeMean : projectedMean;\r\n\r\n    // FORтФЬ├зAR INCERTEZA MтФЬ├мNIMA: Evitar que o cone colapse num traтФЬ┬║o liso na UI\r\n    // MATH FIX: Tornar o spread proporcional тФЬ├б escala total do concurso (0.5% do maxScore)\r\n    // Garante que o cone nтФЬ├║o fique gigante num teste de 10 pontos ou invisтФЬ┬бvel num de 1000.\r\n    const MIN_SPREAD = Math.max(0.5, maxScore * 0.005);\r\n    \r\n    // FIX BUG 2: Prender a mтФЬ┬оdia visual dentro dos limites da prova\r\n    const clampedDisplayMean = Math.max(minScore, Math.min(maxScore, displayMean));\r\n    \r\n    const wasVisualCIClamped = (rawHigh - rawLow < MIN_SPREAD);\r\n    if (wasVisualCIClamped) {\r\n        // FIX BUG 6: CompensaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o assimтФЬ┬оtrica.\r\n        // Se bater no teto, o recuo do MIN_SPREAD tem de ser integralmente descontado do piso,\r\n        // garantindo que o spread final nunca seja menor que MIN_SPREAD.\r\n        rawLow = Math.max(minScore, clampedDisplayMean - MIN_SPREAD / 2);\r\n        rawHigh = Math.min(maxScore, clampedDisplayMean + MIN_SPREAD / 2);\r\n\r\n        if (rawHigh === maxScore) {\r\n            rawLow = Math.max(minScore, maxScore - MIN_SPREAD);\r\n        } else if (rawLow === minScore) {\r\n            rawHigh = Math.min(maxScore, minScore + MIN_SPREAD);\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        if (rawLow > rawHigh) {\r\n            rawLow = minScore;\r\n            rawHigh = maxScore;\r\n        }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    const displayLow = rawLow;\r\n    const displayHigh = rawHigh;\r\n\r\n    // BUGFIX M3: Sync the exported 'sd' with the visual clamp to avoid mathematical inconsistency\r\n    // for external consumers of the statistical JSON.\r\n    // BUG-AUDIT-10 FIX: Usar o T-multiplier dinтФЬ├│mico em vez do hardcode 3.92 (=2тФЬ├╣1.96).\r\n    // Para N pequeno o CI usa T(df) >> 1.96, e dividir por 3.92 inflava o SD visual ~3x.\r\n    const effectiveNForSD = Math.max(1, historyLength || 1);\r\n    const tMultiplierForSD = getConfidenceMultiplier(effectiveNForSD, { allowFractional: true });\r\n    const visualSD = wasVisualCIClamped\r\n        ? (rawHigh - rawLow) / (tMultiplierForSD * 2) \r\n        : projectedSD;\r\n\r\n    // CORREтФЬ├зтФЬ├вO: A probabilidade analтФЬ┬бtica usa safeMean (nтФЬ├║o muParam) para consistтФЬ┬мncia.\r\n    // muParam тФЬ┬о deslocado para compensar o viтФЬ┬оs de truncagem na AMOSTRAGEM,\r\n    // mas a fтФЬтФВrmula analтФЬ┬бtica P(X ├Ф├л├С target | X ├Ф├к├к [min,max]) usa тХмтХЭ original.\r\n    const phiMin    = normalCDF_complement((minScore - safeMean) / safeSD); \r\n    const phiMax    = normalCDF_complement((maxScore - safeMean) / safeSD); \r\n    const phiTarget = normalCDF_complement((effectiveTarget - safeMean) / safeSD); \r\n    \r\n    // CORREтФЬ├зтФЬ├вO: Prevenir a anulaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o catastrтФЬтФВfica (Underflow) em caudas severamente truncadas,\r\n    // garantindo que a matemтФЬ├нtica analтФЬ┬бtica sobrevive a amostras estatisticamente extremas.\r\n    const rawTruncNormFactor = phiMin - phiMax;\r\n    const isUnderflowStress = rawTruncNormFactor < 1e-15;\r\n    \r\n    let truncNormFactor = rawTruncNormFactor;\r\n    if (isUnderflowStress) {\r\n        // Adiciona escape empтФЬ┬бrico absoluto: se a variтФЬ├│ncia convergir para zero na borda,\r\n        // forтФЬ┬║a um fator nominal e delega a decisтФЬ├║o para o motor empтФЬ┬бrico de Monte Carlo\r\n        const zScoreMin = safeSD > 0 ? (minScore - muParam) / safeSD : 0;\r\n        const extremeFactor = Math.exp(-0.5 * zScoreMin * zScoreMin) / (Math.abs(zScoreMin) + 1e-6);\r\n        truncNormFactor = Number.isFinite(extremeFactor) && extremeFactor > 1e-15 ? extremeFactor : 1e-6;\r\n    }\r\n    const clampedPhiTarget = Math.max(phiMax, Math.min(phiMin, phiTarget));\r\n\r\n    let analyticalProbability;\r\n    if (effectiveTarget >= maxScore) {\r\n        analyticalProbability = 0;\r\n    } else if (effectiveTarget <= minScore) {\r\n        analyticalProbability = 100;\r\n    } else {\r\n        // CORREтФЬ├зтФЬ├вO: Se houve stress de underflow (valores atтФЬтФВmicos irreais),\r\n        // abdicamos do integral analтФЬ┬бtico para nтФЬ├║o gerar falsos Zeros (0/1e-15)\r\n        // e confiamos 100% no motor de Monte Carlo bruto (EmpтФЬ┬бrico).\r\n        analyticalProbability = isUnderflowStress \r\n            ? empiricalProbability \r\n            : ((clampedPhiTarget - phiMax) / truncNormFactor) * 100; \r\n    }\r\n    const finalAnalyticalProbability = analyticalProbability;\r\n\r\n    const finiteEmpiricalProbability = Number.isFinite(bayesEmpiricalProbability) ? bayesEmpiricalProbability : 0;\r\n    const finiteAnalyticalProbability = Number.isFinite(finalAnalyticalProbability) ? finalAnalyticalProbability : 0;\r\n    const empiricalVsAnalyticalGap = Math.abs(finiteEmpiricalProbability - finiteAnalyticalProbability);\r\n    const lowSimulation = safeSimulations < 1200;\r\n    const highTruncationStress = truncNormFactor < 1e-6;\r\n    const pHat = finiteEmpiricalProbability / 100;\r\n    const empiricalStdErr = Math.sqrt(Math.max(1e-12, (pHat * (1 - pHat)) / Math.max(1, safeSimulations))) * 100;\r\n\r\n    // [AUDIT-FIX-03] FusтФЬ├║o adaptativa avanтФЬ┬║ada (empтФЬ┬бrico + analтФЬ┬бtico):\r\n    // O \"PadrтФЬ├║o Ouro\" para confianтФЬ┬║a total no Monte Carlo de cauda тФЬ┬о alto.\r\n    const GOLD_STANDARD_SIMS = 15000;\r\n\r\n    // ConfianтФЬ┬║a varia suavemente dependendo do volume real processado frente ao PadrтФЬ├║o Ouro\r\n    const empiricalConfidence = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, safeSimulations / GOLD_STANDARD_SIMS));\r\n    \r\n    const truncationPenalty = highTruncationStress ? 0.55 : 1;\r\n    const uncertaintyScaledGap = empiricalVsAnalyticalGap / Math.max(1, empiricalStdErr * 2.2);\r\n    const disagreementPenalty = Math.max(0.35, 1 - (uncertaintyScaledGap / 6));\r\n    \r\n    // O peso ANALтФЬ├мTICO responde verdadeiramente ao poder computacional:\r\n    // cai conforme a confianтФЬ┬║a EMPтФЬ├мRICA sobe.\r\n    const analyticalWeight = Math.min(0.9, Math.max(0.05, (1 - empiricalConfidence) * truncationPenalty * disagreementPenalty));\r\n\r\n    const blendedProbability = (finiteAnalyticalProbability * analyticalWeight)\r\n        + (finiteEmpiricalProbability * (1 - analyticalWeight));\r\n    const recommendedProbability = blendedProbability;\r\n\r\n    // === NEW: Rich Diagnostics for Transparency ===\r\n    const diagnostics = {\r\n      simulationCount: safeSimulations,\r\n      empiricalStdErr: Number(empiricalStdErr.toFixed(3)),\r\n      analyticalWeight: Number(analyticalWeight.toFixed(3)),\r\n      rhoUsed: null, // filled by caller when adaptive\r\n      effectiveN: Math.max(1, historyLength || safeSimulations / 10),\r\n      shrinkageApplied: null, // populated upstream\r\n      volatilitySources: {\r\n        withinSubject: Number(safeSD.toFixed(2)),\r\n        betweenSubjectContribution: 0\r\n      },\r\n      convergence: {\r\n        targetSE: TARGET_PROB_SE,\r\n        achievedSE: Number(empiricalStdErr.toFixed(4)),\r\n        sufficient: empiricalStdErr < TARGET_PROB_SE * 1.5\r\n      },\r\n      policy: lowSimulation ? 'low_sample' : (highTruncationStress ? 'truncated' : 'standard')\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    return {\r\n        simulationCount: safeSimulations,\r\n        probability: finiteEmpiricalProbability,\r\n        analyticalProbability: finiteAnalyticalProbability,\r\n        recommendedProbability,\r\n        probabilityPolicy: lowSimulation\r\n            ? 'blended_low_sample_policy'\r\n            : (highTruncationStress ? 'blended_truncated_policy' : 'blended_adaptive_policy'),\r\n        analyticalWeight,\r\n        empiricalStdErr,\r\n        empiricalProbabilityRaw: empiricalProbability,\r\n        empiricalProbabilityBayes: finiteEmpiricalProbability,\r\n        mean: (bayesianCI ? safeMean : displayMean),\r\n        sd: projectedSD,\r\n        sdVisual: visualSD,\r\n        sdLeft: Math.max(Math.max((maxScore - minScore) * 0.001, 1e-6), empMedian - rawLeft),\r\n        sdRight: Math.max(Math.max((maxScore - minScore) * 0.001, 1e-6), rawRight - empMedian),\r\n        ci95StatLow: statisticalCi95Low,\r\n        ci95StatHigh: statisticalCi95High,\r\n        ci95Low: displayLow,\r\n        ci95High: displayHigh,\r\n        ci95VisualLow: displayLow,\r\n        ci95VisualHigh: displayHigh,\r\n        ci95VisualClamped: wasVisualCIClamped,\r\n        currentMean: (currentMean ?? safeMean),\r\n        projectedMean,\r\n        projectedSD,\r\n        kdeData: generateKDE(allScores, displayMean, projectedSD, safeSimulations, minScore, maxScore),\r\n        drift: 0,\r\n        volatility: safeSD,\r\n        minScore,\r\n        maxScore,\r\n        method: bayesianCI ?
