85;\r\n            const collectedMetrics = [];\r\n\r\n            const result = getSuggestedFocus(\r\n                data.categories,\r\n                data.simuladoRows || [],\r\n                data.studyLogs || [],\r\n                {\r\n                    user: data.user,\r\n                    targetScore,\r\n                    maxScore: data.maxScore ?? 100,\r\n                    calibrationHistoryByCategory: calibrationHistoryRef.current,\r\n                    flashcardDecks: flashcardDecks,\r\n                    flashcardDue,\r\n                    onCalibrationMetric: (metric) => collectedMetrics.push(metric),\r\n                    // Pass global MC stats for richer integration (see analysis of Coach + MC)\r\n                    globalMcStats: mcStats,\r\n                    config: {\r\n                        MC_ENABLE_ADAPTIVE_CALIBRATION: data?.settings?.adaptiveCalibrationEnabled !== false\r\n                    }\r\n                }\r\n            );\r\n\r\n            // BEST: enrich the suggestion with global MC context for the UI\r\n            if (result && mcStats && mcStats.projectedMean != null) {\r\n                result.globalMcContext = {\r\n                    projectedMean: Number(mcStats.projectedMean.toFixed(1)),\r\n                    probability: mcStats.probability != null ? Number(mcStats.probability.toFixed(1)) : null,\r\n                    source: 'useMonteCarloStats'\r\n                };\r\n            }\r\n            setSuggestedFocus(result);\r\n            setIsAnalyzing(false);\r\n\r\n            if (collectedMetrics.length > 0) {\r\n                metricsTimer = setTimeout(() => {\r\n                    collectedMetrics.forEach((metric, i) => {\r\n                        const t = setTimeout(() => persistCalibrationMetric(metric), i * 600);\r\n                        nestedTimeouts.push(t);\r\n                    });\r\n                }, 1000); // Cooldown de 1s para deixar o dashboard respirar entre anтФЬ├нlises\r\n            }\r\n        }, 0);\r\n\r\n        return () => {\r\n            clearTimeout(analysisTimer);\r\n            if (metricsTimer) clearTimeout(metricsTimer);\r\n            nestedTimeouts.forEach(clearTimeout);\r\n        };\r\n    }, [\r\n        isHydrated,\r\n        data?.categories, \r\n        data?.simuladoRows, \r\n        data?.studyLogs, \r\n        data?.user, \r\n        data?.maxScore, \r\n        data?.settings?.adaptiveCalibrationEnabled,\r\n        userProfile?.targetProbability,\r\n        flashcardDue,\r\n        persistCalibrationMetric\r\n    ]);\r\n\r\n    useEffect(() => {\r\n        if (typeof projectedScore === 'number' && !Number.isNaN(projectedScore) && projectedScore !== lastPushedScoreRef.current) {\r\n            if (lastPushedScoreRef.current === null || Math.abs(projectedScore - lastPushedScoreRef.current) > 0.01) {\r\n                lastPushedScoreRef.current = projectedScore;\r\n                const timer = setTimeout(() => {\r\n                    if (updateCoachScore) updateCoachScore(projectedScore);\r\n                }, 0);\r\n                return () => clearTimeout(timer);\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n    }, [projectedScore, updateCoachScore]);\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n    const handleChangeTab = useCallback((tab) => {\r\n        setActiveTab(tab === 'analytics' ? 'analytics' : 'insights');\r\n    }, []);\r\n\r\n    const handleGenerateGoals = useCallback(() => {\r\n        if (!data?.categories || coachLoading) return;\r\n        setCoachLoading(true);\r\n        if (timeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current);\r\n        timeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {\r\n            const targetScore = userProfile?.targetProbability ?? 85;\r\n            const collectedMetrics = [];\r\n\r\n            const newTasks = generateDailyGoals(\r\n                data.categories,\r\n                data.simuladoRows || [],\r\n                data.studyLogs || [],\r\n                {\r\n                    user: data.user,\r\n                    targetScore,\r\n                    maxScore: data.maxScore ?? 100,\r\n                    calibrationHistoryByCategory: calibrationHistoryRef.current, // FIX: Uso de Ref para evitar Stale Closure\r\n                    onCalibrationMetric: (metric) => collectedMetrics.push(metric),\r\n                    config: {\r\n                        MC_ENABLE_ADAPTIVE_CALIBRATION: data?.settings?.adaptiveCalibrationEnabled !== false\r\n                    }\r\n                }\r\n            );\r\n            \r\n            if (newTasks.length) {\r\n                setData(prev => { if(prev) prev.coachPlan = newTasks; });\r\n                showToast('SugestтФЬ├Бes geradas!', 'success');\r\n            } else {\r\n                showToast('Nenhuma sugestтФЬ├║o necessтФЬ├нria.', 'info');\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            collectedMetrics.forEach((metric, i) => {\r\n                const t = setTimeout(() => persistCalibrationMetric(metric), i * 600);\r\n                if (window._coachGenerationTimeouts) window._coachGenerationTimeouts.push(t);\r\n            });\r\n            setCoachLoading(false);\r\n            // LOGIC-TIMEOUT-NULL FIX: zerar a ref apтФЬтФВs a execuтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o para nтФЬ├║o manter\r\n            // um ID de timeout expirado que mascararia novos agendamentos.\r\n            timeoutRef.current = null;\r\n        }, 1500);\r\n    }, [data, coachLoading, setData, showToast, persistCalibrationMetric, userProfile?.targetProbability]);\r\n\r\n    const handleClearHistory = useCallback(() => {\r\n        setData(prev => { if (prev) prev.coachPlan = []; });\r\n        useAppStore.getState().updateCoachPlanner({ mon: [], tue: [], wed: [], thu: [], fri: [], sat: [], sun: [] });\r\n    }, [setData]);\r\n\r\n    useEffect(() => {\r\n        window._coachGenerationTimeouts = [];\r\n        return () => {\r\n            if (timeoutRef.current) {\r\n                clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current);\r\n                timeoutRef.current = null;\r\n            }\r\n            if (window._coachGenerationTimeouts) {\r\n                window._coachGenerationTimeouts.forEach(clearTimeout);\r\n                window._coachGenerationTimeouts = [];\r\n            }\r\n        };\r\n    }, []);\r\n\r\n    if (isAnalyzing || !data || !data.categories) {\r\n        return (\r\n            <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-[60vh] gap-4\">\r\n                <div className=\"relative\">\r\n                    <div className=\"w-16 h-16 border-4 border-indigo-500/20 border-t-indigo-500 rounded-full animate-spin\" />\r\n                    <Brain className=\"absolute inset-0 m-auto text-indigo-500 animate-pulse\" size={24} />\r\n                </div>\r\n                <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center\">\r\n                    <span className=\"text-white font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-xs\">Sincronizando Redes Neurais</span>\r\n                    <span className=\"text-slate-500 text-[10px] mt-1 uppercase font-bold animate-pulse\">Processando Probabilidades...</span>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n        );\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return (\r\n        <PageErrorBoundary pageName=\"Coach\">\r\n            <div className=\"max-w-full mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8 pb-32\">\r\n                <div className=\"relative z-50 flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center justify-between gap-6 mb-10\">\r\n                    <PageHeader \r\n                        title=\"AnтФЬ├нlise do Coach\" \r\n                        description=\"Mentor estatтФЬ┬бstico processando seu desempenho para otimizar sua aprovaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o.\"\r\n                    />\r\n                    \r\n                    <div className=\"relative z-[60] flex flex-wrap sm:flex-nowrap items-center gap-3 sm:gap-4 bg-slate-900/50 border border-white/10 p-2 sm:p-3 rounded-3xl backdrop-blur-xl w-full md:w-auto shadow-inner\">\r\n                        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 sm:gap-4 px-2\">\r\n                            <QuickStat label=\"Volatilidade\" value={`${normalizedVolatility.toFixed(1)}pp`} color=\"text-rose-400\" icon={<Zap size={14} />} />\r\n                            <div className=\"w-px h-6 bg-white/10\" />\r\n                            <QuickStat\r\n                                label=\"TendтФЬ┬мncia\"\r\n                                value={`${((drift * 30) / Math.max(1, Number(currentMaxScore) || 1) * 100).toFixed(1)}pp`}\r\n                                color=\"text-emerald-400\"\r\n                                icon={<ArrowUpRight size={14} />}\r\n                            />\r\n                            <div className=\"w-px h-6 bg-white/10\" />\r\n                            <QuickStat label=\"Simulados\" value={totalSimulados} color=\"text-indigo-400\" icon={<Dna size={14} />} />\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div className=\"hidden sm:block w-px h-6 bg-white/10\" />\r\n                        <MonteCarloDebugger stats={mcStats} />\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n\r\n                <AnimatePresence>\r\n                    <GovernanceBanner data={data} />\r\n                </AnimatePresence>\r\n\r\n                <div className=\"space-y-10\">\r\n                    <div className=\"w-full\">\r\n                        <CoachMenuNav activeTab={safeActiveTab} onChangeTab={handleChangeTab} isPremium={isPremium} />\r\n\r\n                        <Motion.div \r\n                            key={safeActiveTab}\r\n                            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}\r\n                            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\r\n                            transition={{ duration: 0.25, ease: \"easeOut\" }}\r\n                            className=\"min-h-[200px]\"\r\n                        >\r\n                            <div\r\n                                role=\"tabpanel\"\r\n                                id=\"coach-panel-insights\"\r\n                                aria-labelledby=\"coach-tab-insights\"\r\n                                tabIndex={safeActiveTab === 'insights' ? 0 : -1}\r\n                                hidden={safeActiveTab !== 'insights'}\r\n                            >\r\n                                {safeActiveTab === 'insights' && (\r\n                                    <>\r\n                                        {flashcardDue > 0 && (\r\n                                            <div className=\"mb-3 flex items-center gap-3 rounded-2xl border border-amber-500/20 bg-amber-500/5 px-4 py-3 text-sm\">\r\n                                                <BookOpen className=\"text-amber-400\" size={18} />\r\n                                                <div className=\"flex-1 text-amber-200\">\r\n                                                    <span className=\"font-semibold\">{flashcardDue} flashcards</span> pendentes para hoje. SRS melhora retenтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o e o modelo.\r\n                                                </div>\r\n                                                <button\r\n                                                    onClick={() => navigate('/flashcards')}\r\n                                                    className=\"rounded-xl border border-amber-500/30 bg-amber-500/10 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-bold text-amber-200 hover:bg-amber-500/20 transition\"\r\n                                                >\r\n                                                    FLASHCARDS\r\n                                                </button>\r\n                                            </div>\r\n                                        )}\r\n\r\n                                        {/* Visual global MC context */}\r\n                                        {suggestedFocus?.globalProjectedMean != null && (\r\n                                            <div className=\"mb-3 flex items-center gap-2 MC:</span>\r\n                                                <span className=\"font-mono text-base font-bold text-emerald-200\">{suggestedFocus.globalProjectedMean}%</span>\r\n                                                <span className=\"text-emerald-400/60\">contexto global aplicado</span>\r\n                                            </div>\r\n                                        )}\r\n                                        <AICoachView \r\n                                            suggestedFocus={suggestedFocus}\r\n                                            onGenerateGoals={handleGenerateGoals}\r\n                                            loading={coachLoading}\r\n                                            onClearHistory={handleClearHistory}\r\n                                        />\r\n                                    </>\r\n                                )}\r\n                            </div>\r\n\r\n                            <div\r\n                                role=\"tabpanel\"\r\n                                id=\"coach-panel-analytics\"\r\n                                aria-labelledby=\"coach-tab-analytics\"\r\n                                tabIndex={safeActiveTab === 'analytics' ? 0 : -1}\r\n                                hidden={safeActiveTab !== 'analytics'}\r\n                            >\r\n                                {safeActiveTab === 'analytics' && <RaioXDashboard data={data} />}\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        </Motion.div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n        </PageErrorBoundary>\r\n    );\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction QuickStat({ label, value, color, icon }) {\r\n    return (\r\n        <div className=\"flex flex-col min-w-[78px] sm:min-w-[80px] px-1\">\r\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-0.5 opacity-70\">\r\n                <span className={color}>{icon}</span>\r\n                <span className=\"text-[8px] font-black text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-[0.25em]\">{label}</span>\r\n            </div>\r\n            <span className={`text-base font-black ${color} tracking-tighter tabular-nums`}>{value}</span>\r\n        </div>\r\n    );\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction StatRow({ label, value, trend, color }) {\r\n    return (\r\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-b border-white/5 last:border-0\">\r\n            <span className=\"text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider\">{label}</span>\r\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\r\n                <span className={`text-xs font-black ${color}`}>{value}</span>\r\n                {trend === 'up' && <ArrowUpRight size={12} className=\"text-emerald-500\" />}\r\n                {trend === 'down' && <AlertCircle size={12} className=\"text-rose-500\" />}\r\n            </div>\r\n        </div>\r\n    );\r\n}\r\n\r\nconst GovernanceBanner = React.memo(function GovernanceBanner({ data }) {\r\n    const ops = data?.calibrationOps || {};\r\n    const degradedCount = Object.values(ops).filter(o => o.degraded).length;\r\n\r\n    if (degradedCount === 0) return null;\r\n\r\n    return (\r\n        <Motion.div \r\n            layout\r\n            initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}\r\n            animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}\r\n            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}\r\n            className=\"mb-6 p-4 rounded-3xl bg-rose-500/5 border border-rose-500/30 flex items-center justify-between gap-4 overflow-hidden shadow-sm\"\r\n        >\r\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4\">\r\n                <div className=\"w-10 h-10 rounded-2xl bg-rose-500/15 flex items-center justify-center text-rose-400 border border-rose-500/20\">\r\n                    <AlertCircle size={20} />\r\n                </div>\r\n                <div>\r\n                    <h4 className=\"text-sm font-black text-rose-200 uppercase tracking-tight\">Alerta de GovernanтФЬ┬║a</h4>\r\n                    <p className=\"text-[10px] text-rose-300/80 font-medium uppercase tracking-widest\">\r\n                        Detectamos <span className=\"text-rose-400 font-black\">{degradedCount}</span> categorias com calibraтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o degradada.\r\n                    </p>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n            <div className=\"hidden sm:block text-right\">\r\n                <p className=\"text-[9px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-black tracking-widest leading-tight\">\r\n                    O Coach estтФЬ├н aplicando<br/>ajustes conservadores.\r\n                </p>\r\n            </div>\r\n        </Motion.div>\r\n    );\r\n});\r\n\r\nfunction RaioXDashboard({ data }) {\r\n    const ops = data?.calibrationOps || {};\r\n    const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');\r\n\r\n    const toFiniteNumber = (value, fallback = 0) => {\r\n        const n = Number(value);\r\n        return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const toPercentLabel = (value) => {\r\n        const n = Number(value);\r\n        if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return '-';\r\n        return `${Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(n)))}%`;\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const sortedLogs = useMemo(() => {\r\n        const source = Array.isArray(data?.calibrationAuditLog) ? data.calibrationAuditLog : [];\r\n        return [...source].sort((a, b) => toFiniteNumber(b?.timestamp) - toFiniteNumber(a?.timestamp));\r\n    }, [data?.calibrationAuditLog]);\r\n\r\n    const filteredLogs = useMemo(() => (sortedLogs\r\n        .filter(log => filter === 'all' || (filter === 'degraded' && Boolean(log?.degraded)))\r\n        .slice(0, 50)), [sortedLogs, filter]);\r\n\r\n    const latestWithReliability = sortedLogs.find(log => Array.isArray(log?.reliability) && log.reliability.length > 0);\r\n    const eceValues = sortedLogs.map(log => Number(log?.ece)).filter(Number.isFinite);\r\n    const avgEce = eceValues.length ? (eceValues.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / eceValues.length) : null;\r\n    const categorySeriesMap = sortedLogs.reduce((acc, log) => {\r\n        const cat = log?.categoryName || 'Categoria';\r\n        if (!acc[cat]) acc[cat] = [];\r\n        acc[cat].push({\r\n            ts: toFiniteNumber(log?.timestamp),\r\n            brier: toFiniteNumber(log?.avgBrier),\r\n            ece: toFiniteNumber(log?.ece)\r\n        });\r\n        return acc;\r\n    }, {});\r\n    const categoryNames = Object.keys(categorySeriesMap);\r\n    const [seriesCategory, setSeriesCategory] = useState(() => categoryNames[0] || '');\r\n    // BUG-07 FIX: Keep selected category valid when data changes\r\n    const effectiveCategory = categoryNames.includes(seriesCategory) ? seriesCategory : (categoryNames[0] || '');\r\n    const temporalSeries = effectiveCategory\r\n        ? [...categorySeriesMap[effectiveCategory]].sort((a, b) => a.ts - b.ts).slice(-12)\r\n        : [];\r\n\r\n    return (\r\n        <div className=\"space-y-12 animate-fade-in\">\r\n            <div className=\"grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-8\">\r\n                <div className=\"p-2\">\r\n                    <h3 className=\"text-[11px] font-black text-slate-500/80 uppercase tracking-[0.2em] mb-5 flex items-center gap-2\">\r\n                        <ShieldCheck size={14} className=\"text-emerald-500/80\" />\r\n                        Status de CalibraтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o\r\n                    </h3>\r\n                    <div className=\"space-y-3\">\r\n                        {Object.entries(ops).map(([id, op]) => (\r\n                            <div key={id} className=\"p-3 rounded-xl bg-black/20 border border-white/5 flex items-center justify-between px-4\">\r\n                                <div className=\"min-w-0 flex-1\">\r\n                                    <p className=\"text-xs font-bold text-white truncate\">{displaySubject(op.categoryName || id)}</p>\r\n                                    <p className=\"text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-black tracking-tighter pl-2.5\">CalibraтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o 7d (Brier): {Number.isFinite(Number(op.avgBrier7d)) ? Number(op.avgBrier7d).toFixed(3) : \"N/A\"}</p>\r\n                                </div>\r\n                                <div className={`shrink-0 ml-4 px-3 py-1 rounded-xl text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest ${op.degraded ? 'bg-rose-500/20 text-rose-400 border border-rose-500/30' : 'bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-400 border border-emerald-500/20'}`}>\r\n                                    {op.degraded ? 'Degradado' : 'EstтФЬ├нvel'}\r\n                                </div>\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        ))}\r\n                        {Object.keys(ops).length === 0 && (\r\n                            <div className=\"py-8 text-center space-y-2\">\r\n                                <p className=\"text-[10px] text-slate-600 font-black uppercase tracking-widest\">Amostra tтФЬ┬оcnica insuficiente</p>\r\n                                <p className=\"text-[9px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-tight max-w-[200px] mx-auto leading-tight\">\r\n                                    Requer <span className=\"text-indigo-400\">3 simulados por matтФЬ┬оria</span> para calibrar.\r\n                                </p>\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        )}\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n\r\n                <div className=\"p-2\">\r\n                    <h3 className=\"text-[11px] font-black text-slate-500/80 uppercase tracking-[0.2em] mb-5 flex items-center gap-2\">\r\n                        <Dna size={14} className=\"text-indigo-500/80\" />\r\n                        DNA do HistтФЬтФВrico\r\n                    </h3>\r\n                    <div className=\"p-4 rounded-2xl bg-indigo-500/5 border border-indigo-500/10 text-center\">\r\n                        <p className=\"text-[10px] text-indigo-300/80 leading-relaxed font-medium\">\r\n                            A calibraтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o do modelo combina Brier Score e ECE (Expected Calibration Error). Brier baixo e ECE baixo indicam boa confiabilidade; quando degradam, o Coach aplica reduтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o de confianтФЬ┬║a (shrinkage) para proteger sua estratтФЬ┬оgia.\r\n                        </p>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n            <div className=\"p-2 border-t border-white/5 pt-8\">\r\n                <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-6\">\r\n                    <h3 className=\"text-[11px] font-black text-slate-500/80 uppercase tracking-[0.2em] flex items-center gap-2\">\r\n                        <List size={14} className=\"text-indigo-400/80\" />\r\n                        Log de Auditoria\r\n                    </h3>\r\n                    <div className=\"flex gap-2 bg-slate-900/50 border border-white/5 rounded-xl p-0.5\">\r\n                        <button \r\n                            onClick={() => setFilter('all')}\r\n                            className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest transition-all duration-200 ${filter === 'all' ? 'bg-rose-500/20 text-rose-300' : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200'}`}\r\n                        >\r\n                            Degradados\r\n                        </button>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n                \r\n                <div className=\"overflow-x-auto rounded-2xl border border-white/5 bg-black/10\">\r\n                    <table className=\"w-full text-left\">\r\n                        <thead>\r\n                            <tr className=\"border-b border-white/5\">\r\n                                <th className=\"pb-3 Math.floor(sorted.length * 0.1) : 0;\n    const core = trim > 0 ? sorted.slice(trim, sorted.length - trim) : sorted;\n    // Precision: Kahan for avgBrier\n    const avgBrier = kahanSum(core) / core.length;\n    \n    // A penalidade agora тФЬ┬о baseada no Brier Score, mas o motor deve monitorar Log Loss\n    // para diagnтФЬтФВsticos de \"falsa sensaтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o de domтФЬ┬бnio\" (Entropia).\n    const calibrationPenalty = Math.min(maxPenalty, Math.max(0, avgBrier - baseline));\n    \n    return { avgBrier, calibrationPenalty, sampleSize: finiteScores.length };\n}\n\nexport function computeCalibrationDiagnostics(pairs = [], options = {}) {\n  const bins = Math.max(2, Number(options.bins) || 5);\n  if (!Array.isArray(pairs) || pairs.length === 0) return { ece: 0, mce: 0, reliability: [], brierDecomposition: null };\n\n  const cleanPairs = pairs\n    .map((p) => ({\n      probability: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(p?.probability))),\n      observed: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(p?.observed)))\n    }))\n    .filter((p) => Number.isFinite(p.probability) && Number.isFinite(p.observed));\n  if (cleanPairs.length === 0) return { ece: 0, mce: 0, reliability: [], brierDecomposition: null };\n\n  const sorted = [...cleanPairs].sort((a, b) => a.probability - b.probability);\n  let ece = 0;\n  let mce = 0;\n  const reliability = [];\n  const overallObserved = kahanSum(cleanPairs.map(p => p.observed)) / cleanPairs.length;\n  let relTerm = 0;\n  let resTerm = 0;\n  \n  // [FIX 3] Usar bins de largura fixa (Equal Width) para evitar aglomeraтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o visual\n  for (let i = 0; i < bins; i++) {\n    const binMin = i / bins;\n    const binMax = (i + 1) / bins;\n    \n    // Filtra pares que caem dentro deste intervalo de probabilidade\n    const slice = sorted.filter(p => p.probability >= binMin && p.probability < (i === bins - 1 ? 1.01 : binMax));\n    \n    if (slice.length === 0) continue;\n    \n    const meanPred = kahanSum(slice.map(p => p.probability)) / slice.length;\n    const observedRate = kahanSum(slice.map(p => p.observed)) / slice.length;\n    const gap = Math.abs(meanPred - observedRate);\n    const weight = slice.length / cleanPairs.length;\n    ece += weight * gap;\n    mce = Math.max(mce, gap);\n    relTerm += weight * ((meanPred - observedRate) ** 2);\n    resTerm += weight * ((observedRate - overallObserved) ** 2);\n    reliability.push({ bin: i + 1, count: slice.length, meanPred, observedRate, gap });\n  }\n  const uncertainty = overallObserved * (1 - overallObserved);\n  return {\n    ece,\n    mce,\n    reliability,\n    brierDecomposition: {\n      reliability: relTerm,\n      resolution: resTerm,\n      uncertainty\n    }\n  };\n}\n\nexport function shrinkProbabilityToNeutral(probabilityPct, penalty, neutralPct = 50, maxAppliedPenalty = 0.5) {\n    const p = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Number(probabilityPct) || 0));\n    const limit = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(maxAppliedPenalty) || 0.5));\n    const k = Math.max(0, Math.min(limit, Number(penalty) || 0));\n    const neutral = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Number(neutralPct) || 50));\n    return p * (1 - k) + neutral * k;\n}\n\n/**\n * NEW: Record a Monte Carlo prediction outcome for future calibration.\n * Stores lightweight events that can be used for walk-forward analysis.\n */\nexport function recordPredictionEvent(storeUpdateFn, prediction) {\n  // prediction: { timestamp, probability, observed, targetScore, sims, category, effectiveN? }\n  if (typeof storeUpdateFn !== 'function') return;\n  const event = {\n    timestamp: prediction.timestamp || Date.now(),\n    probability: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(prediction.probability) || 0)),\n    observed: prediction.observed != null ? (prediction.observed ? 1 : 0) : null,\n    targetScore: prediction.targetScore,\n    sims: prediction.sims || 5000,\n    category: prediction.category || 'global',\n    effectiveN: prediction.effectiveN || null\n  };\n  // The caller is responsible for pushing to a contest.calibrationEvents array\n  // We just validate and return a clean event\n  return event;\n}\n\n/**\n * Aggregate calibration events into metrics + trend.\n * Supports walk-forward style analysis.\n */\nexport function computeCalibrationSummary(events = [], options = {}) {\n  const clean = (events || []).filter(e => \n    Number.isFinite(e?.probability) && \n    (e?.observed === 0 || e?.observed === 1)\n  );\n\n  if (clean.length < 3) {\n    return { n: clean.length, ece: 0, avgBrier: 0, reliability: [], trend: 'insufficient_data' };\n  }\n\n  const diag = computeCalibrationDiagnostics(clean.map(e => ({ probability: e.probability, observed: e.observed })), { bins: options.bins || 6 });\n\n  const briers = clean.map(e => computeBrierScore(e.probability, e.observed));\n  const avgBrier = kahanSum(briers) / briers.length;\n\n  // Simple trend: compare first half vs second half Brier\n  const mid = Math.floor(clean.length / 2);\n  const firstHalf = briers.slice(0, mid);\n  const secondHalf = briers.slice(mid);\n  const firstAvg = firstHalf.length ? kahanSum(firstHalf) / firstHalf.length : avgBrier;\n  const secondAvg = secondHalf.length ? kahanSum(secondHalf) / secondHalf.length : avgBrier;\n  const trend = secondAvg < firstAvg * 0.92 ? 'improving' : (secondAvg > firstAvg * 1.08 ? 'degrading' : 'stable');\n\n  return {\n    n: clean.length,\n    ece: diag.ece,\n    mce: diag.mce,\n    avgBrier: Number(avgBrier.toFixed(4)),\n    reliability: diag.reliability,\n    trend,\n    brierDecomposition: diag.brierDecomposition\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * NEW: Try to backfill observed values in calibrationEvents using actual simulado results.\n * Matches by category and approximate target.\n * Call this after adding/updating simulados.\n */\nexport function backfillObservedFromSimulados(calibrationEvents = [], simuladoRows = [], categories = [], maxScore = 100) {\n  if (!Array.isArray(calibrationEvents) || !Array.isArray(simuladoRows)) return calibrationEvents;\n\n  const updated = [...calibrationEvents];\n\n  simuladoRows.forEach(row => {\n    const subj = row.subject || row.categoryName;\n    if (!subj) return;\n\n    const score = Number(row.score ?? ((row.correct / row.total) * (row.maxScore || maxScore)));\n    if (!Number.isFinite(score)) return;\n\n    // Find recent global or per-subject predictions that might match this simulado\n    updated.forEach(ev => {\n      if (ev.observed != null) return; // already filled\n      if (!ev.category) return;\n\n      const isMatch = ev.category.toLowerCase().includes(subj.toLowerCase()) ||\n                      subj.toLowerCase().includes(ev.category.toLowerCase());\n\n      if (isMatch && ev.targetScore) {\n        // Simple rule: if the simulado score >= target, it was a \"pass\" for that prediction\n        const passed = score >= Number(ev.targetScore);\n        ev.observed = passed ? 1 : 0;\n        ev.backfilled = true;\n      }\n    });\n  });\n\n  return updated;\n}\n\nexport function computeRollingCalibrationParams(history = [], cfg = {}) {\n  const safeHistory = Array.isArray(history) ? history : [];\n  if (safeHistory.length === 0) {\n    return { baseline: cfg.baseline ?? 0.2, maxPenalty: cfg.maxPenalty ?? 0.3 };\n  }\n  const windowDays = Number(cfg.windowDays) || 60;\n  const cutoff = Date.now() - (windowDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n  const maxSamples = Number(cfg.maxSamples) || 20;\n  const recent = safeHistory\n    .filter(h => Number.isFinite(Number(h?.timestamp)) && Number(h.timestamp) >= cutoff)\n    .sort((a, b) => Number(a.timestamp) - (h.timestamp || now));\n    const w = Math.exp(-LAMBDA_CALIB * age);\n    sumWeightedBrier += (Number(h.avgBrier) || 0) * w;\n    sumCalibWeights += w;\n  });\n  const avgBrier = sumCalibWeights > 0 ? sumWeightedBrier / sumCalibWeights : 0;\n\n  // ESTABILIZADOR DE ESCASSEZ DE DADOS: O fator de confianтФЬ┬║a varia suavemente em direтФЬ┬║тФЬ├║o ao target de 12 amostras\n  const targetSamples = Number(cfg.targetSamples) || 12;\n  const confidenceFactor = Math.min(1, recent.length / targetSamples);\n  \n  // Dynamic baseline with confidence-gating to avoid overreacting on short windows\n  const dynamicBaseline = Math.max(0.12, Math.min(0.25, avgBrier));\n  const defaultBaseline = cfg.baseline ?? 0.2;\n  const baseline = (dynamicBaseline * confidenceFactor) + (defaultBaseline * (1 - confidenceFactor));\n  // Penalty cap also confidence-aware\n  const dynamicMaxPenalty = avgBrier > 0.25 ? 0.35 : 0.25;\n  const defaultMaxPenalty = cfg.maxPenalty ?? 0.3;\n  const maxPenalty = (dynamicMaxPenalty * confidenceFactor) + (defaultMaxPenalty * (1 - confidenceFactor));\n  \n  return { baseline, maxPenalty, confidenceFactor };\n}\n\n\n// Governance Playbook Constants\nexport const CRITICAL_BRIER_THRESHOLD = 0.28;\nexport const HIGH_PENALTY_THRESHOLD = 0.20;\nexport const ALERT_COOLDOWN_MS = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 12; // 12h\n\n\n// -------- Advanced calibration tooling --------\nexport function fitIsotonicCalibration(pairs = []) {\n  const clean = (pairs || [])\n    .map(p => ({ x: Number(p?.probability), y: Number(p?.observed) }))\n    .filter(p => Number.isFinite(p.x) && Number.isFinite(p.y))\n    .map(p => ({ x: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, p.x)), y: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, p.y)), w: 1 }))\n    .sort((a, b) => a.x - b.x);\n  if (clean.length === 0) return [];\n\n  const blocks = clean.map(p => ({ minX: p.x, maxX: p.x, sumWY: p.y, sumW: 1, mean: p.y }));\n  let i = 0;\n  while (i < blocks.length - 1) {\n    if (blocks[i].mean <= blocks[i + 1].mean) { i++; continue; }\n    const merged = {\n      minX: blocks[i].minX,\n      maxX: blocks[i + 1].maxX,\n      sumWY: blocks[i].sumWY + blocks[i + 1].sumWY,\n      sumW: blocks[i].sumW + blocks[i + 1].sumW,\n      mean: 0\n    };\n    merged.mean = merged.sumWY / merged.sumW;\n    blocks.splice(i, 2, merged);\n    if (i > 0) i--;\n  }\n  return blocks.map(b => ({ minX: b.minX, maxX: b.maxX, value: b.mean }));\n}\n\nexport function predictIsotonicProbability(probability01, model = []) {\n  const p = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(probability01) || 0));\n  if (!model || model.length === 0) return p;\n  if (p < model[0].minX) return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(model[0].value) || 0));\n\n  let bestValue = model[0].value;\n  for (const block of model) {\n      if (p >= block.minX) {\n          bestValue = block.value;\n      } else {\n          break; // PassтФЬ├нmos o ponto, ficamos com o тФЬтХСltimo degrau vтФЬ├нlido\n      }\n  }\n  return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(bestValue) || 0));\n}\n\nexport function calibrateWithBBQ(probability01, pairs = [], options = {}) {\n  const p = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(probability01) || 0));\n  const clean = (pairs || [])\n    .map(x => ({ probability: Number(x?.probability), observed: Number(x?.observed) }))\n    .filter(x => Number.isFinite(x.probability) && Number.isFinite(x.observed))\n    .map(x => ({ probability: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x.probability)), observed: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x.observed)) }));\n  if (clean.length < 4) return p;\n\n  const sorted = [...clean].sort((a, b) => a.probability - 0.15), high: Math.min(1, p + 0.15), qHat: 0.15 };\n  }\n  const residuals = clean.map(x => Math.abs(Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x.probability)) - Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x.observed)))).sort((a,b)=>a-b);\n  const n = residuals.length;\n  const safeAlpha = Math.max(0.01, Math.min(0.4, alpha));\n  const qIdx = Math.max(0, Math.min(Math.ceil((1 - import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';

test.describe('Core User Journey', () => {
  test('Dashboard loads correctly and navigation works', async ({ page }) => {
    // Navigate to the app
    await page.goto('/');

    // Wait for the app to hydrate
    await expect(page.locator('#root')).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10000 });
    
    // Handle Local Mode Login Screen
    await page.fill('input[type="email"]', 'test@example.com');
    await page.fill('input[type="password"]', '123456');
    const loginButton = page.locator('button', { hasText: 'ENTRAR' });
    await expect(loginButton).toBeVisible({ timeout: 15000 });
    await loginButton.click();
    
    // Dismiss the welcome screen
    // Since the first ENTRAR button is unmounted, 'text=Entrar' might just match the welcome screen one
    await expect(page.locator('text=Bem-vindo')).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10000 });
    await page.locator('button:has-text("Entrar")').click();

    // Check if the sidebar or main navigation is present (adjust selectors based on actual DOM)
    // Assuming there is a nav element or a sidebar
    const dashboardTitle = page.locator('text=/Sequ├Г┬кncia|Efici├Г┬кncia|Equil├Г┬нbrio|Flashcards/i').first();
    await expect(dashboardTitle).toBeVisible({ timeout: 15000 });

    // Ensure no severe errors exist on the page
    const errorBoundaryMessage = page.locator('text=Algo deu errado');
    await expect(errorBoundaryMessage).toHaveCount(0);
  });
});

export function shouldSkipForMissingBrowser(output = '') {
  return output.includes("Executable doesn't exist")
    || output.includes('Please run the following command to download new browsers');
}

export function resolveStatus({ status, error, output }) {
  if (error) return 1;
  if ((status ?? 1) !== 0 && shouldSkipForMissingBrowser(output)) return 0;
  return status ?? 1;
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, Suspense, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';

import { useAuth } from './context/useAuth';
import { useSubscription } from './hooks/useSubscription';
import { useAppStore, useTemporalStore } from './store/useAppStore';
import { useShallow } from 'zustand/react/shallow';
import { useCloudSync } from './hooks/useCloudSync';
import { useToast } from './hooks/useToast';

import { useGlobalToasts } from './hooks/useGlobalToasts';
import { useLevelUp } from './hooks/useLevelUp';
import { useThemeSync } from './hooks/useThemeSync';
import { parseImportedData } from './utils/backupManager';
import { exportData } from './data/initialData';
import useIdleLogout from './hooks/useIdleLogout';



import './components/Loading.css';

const EMPTY_OBJECT = {};

function MainLayout() {
  const location = useLocation();
  const { currentUser, loading, logout } = useAuth();
  const { isPremium, loading: subLoading } = useSubscription(currentUser);

  const activeContestId = useAppStore(state => state.appState.activeId);

  // Otimiza├Г┬з├Г┬гo: Seletores est├Г┬бveis e granulares para evitar re-renderiza├Г┬з├Г┬╡es massivas
  const contestsMetaSelector = useShallow(state => {
    return Object.keys(state.appState.contests).reduce((acc, key) => {
      acc[key] = state.appState.contests[key]?.contestName || 'Sem nome';
      return acc;
    }, {});
  });
  const contestsMetaList = useAppStore(contestsMetaSelector);

  const headerDataSelector = useShallow(state => {
    const contest = state.appState.contests[activeContestId];
    return {
      exists: !!contest,
      user: contest?.user,
      settings: contest?.settings
    };
  });
  const headerData = useAppStore(headerDataSelector);

  const syncTriggerSelector = useShallow(state => ({
    version: state.appState.version,
    lastUpdated: state.appState.lastUpdated
  }));
  const syncTrigger = useAppStore(syncTriggerSelector);


  const setAppState = useAppStore(state => state.setAppState);
  const switchContest = useAppStore(state => state.switchContest);
  const createNewContest = useAppStore(state => state.createNewContest);
  const deleteContest = useAppStore(state => state.deleteContest);
  const updateUserName = useAppStore(state => state.updateUserName);
  const undo = useTemporalStore(state => state.undo);

  const importTimeoutRef = useRef(null);

  // Custom Hooks para l├Г┬│gica global
    const { toasts, removeToast } = useGlobalToasts();
    const { levelUpData, clearLevelUp } = useLevelUp();
    const showToast = useToast();

  // --- AUTO-LOGOUT (60 MIN INACTIVITY) ---
  // BUG-FIX: Increased from 20 to 60 to safely handle Pomodoro sessions (25m + break)
  useIdleLogout(logout, 60 * 60 * 1000);

  // Handle cross-tab sync using real-time listener inside sync context
  const [showHelpGuide, setShowHelpGuide] = useState(false);
  const [isSidebarOpen, setIsSidebarOpen] = useState(false);
  const [sidebarCollapsed, setSidebarCollapsed] = useState(true);
  const [trashOpen, setTrashOpen] = useState(false);
  const rescueAttemptsRef = useRef(0);
  
  // Controle da tela de Boas-Vindas (Premium) - Aparece 1x por sess├Г┬гo (login)
  // ├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм ESTADO DA TELA DE BOAS-VINDAS ├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм
  const [showWelcome, setShowWelcome] = useState(() => {
      // Verifica se a tela de boas-vindas j├Г┬б foi vista nesta sess├Г┬гo
      const hasSeen = sessionStorage.getItem('hasSeenWelcomeScreen');
      return !hasSeen;
  });

  const handleDismissWelcome = useCallback(() => {
      sessionStorage.setItem('hasSeenWelcomeScreen', 'true');
      setShowWelcome(false);
  }, []);

  // Garante que se o usu├Г┬бrio fizer logout (voltar para a tela de login), 
  // o estado reseta para mostrar o WelcomeScreen no pr├Г┬│ximo login.
  useEffect(() => {
      if (!loading && !currentUser) {
          sessionStorage.removeItem('hasSeenWelcomeScreen');
          // eslint-disable-next-line
          setShowWelcome(true);
      }
  }, [currentUser, loading]);
  // ├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм

  // Flag reativa da Store para garantir hidrata├Г┬з├Г┬гo at├Г┬┤mica
  const isStoreHydrated = useAppStore(state => state.appState.isHydrated);

  // Auto-save pipeline
  const { cloudStatus, cloudError, isSyncing: isCloudSyncing, hasConflict, forcePullCloud } = useCloudSync(
    isStoreHydrated ? currentUser : null,
    setAppState,
    showToast,
    syncTrigger // Pass trigger to notify hook of changes (version/lastUpdated)
  );

  // --- THEME SYNC ---
  useThemeSync(headerData.settings?.darkMode);


  // --- RESCUE NOTIFICATION & DASHBOARD RESCUE ---
  useEffect(() => {
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.__ULTRA_RESCUE_SUCCESS) {
      showToast('Dados de "Direito" recuperados do armazenamento profundo! ├░┼╕тАЩ┼╜├░┼╕тАЬ┼б', 'success');
      delete window.__ULTRA_RESCUE_SUCCESS;
    }

    // Reseta contador ao retornar para estado saud├Г┬бvel
    if (isStoreHydrated && headerData.exists) {
      rescueAttemptsRef.current = 0;
    }

    let rescueTimer = null;
    let resetTimer = null;

    if (isStoreHydrated && !headerData.exists && rescueAttemptsRef.current < 3) {
      const keys = Object.keys(contestsMetaList || {});
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        console.warn('[Rescue] Concurso ativo inv├Г┬бlido. Selecionando fallback:', keys[0]);
        rescueAttemptsRef.current += 1;
        
        rescueTimer = setTimeout(() => switchContest(keys[0]), 100);
        
        // Reset ap├Г┬│s 30s de estabilidade
        resetTimer = setTimeout(() => { 
          rescueAttemptsRef.current = 0; 
        }, 30000);
      }
    }

    return () => {
      if (rescueTimer) clearTimeout(rescueTimer);
      if (resetTimer) clearTimeout(resetTimer);
    };
  }, [showToast, isStoreHydrated, headerData.exists, contestsMetaList, switchContest]);

  const cloudStatusHeader = React.useMemo(() => ({
    status: cloudStatus,
    error: cloudError,
    syncing: isCloudSyncing,
    hasConflict,
    forcePull: forcePullCloud
  }), [cloudStatus, cloudError, isCloudSyncing, hasConflict, forcePullCloud]);

  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (importTimeoutRef.current) {
        clearTimeout(importTimeoutRef.current);
        importTimeoutRef.current = null;
      }
    };
  }, []);

  // Global Handlers
  const handleUndo = useCallback(() => {
    undo();
    showToast('A├Г┬з├Г┬гo desfeita! ├втАа┬й├п┬╕┬П', 'info');
  }, [undo, showToast]);

  const handleImport = useCallback((event) => {
    const file = event.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    event.target.value = '';

    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (e) => {
      showToast('A processar backup... ├в┬П┬│', 'info');

      // Joga o processamento pesado para o final da fila de eventos, 
      // deixando a anima├Г┬з├Г┬гo do Toast ocorrer fluida.
      if (importTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(importTimeoutRef.current);
      importTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
        try {
          const currentAppState = useAppStore.getState().appState;
          const result = parseImportedData(e.target.result, currentAppState);
          setAppState(result.data);
          showToast('Backup restaurado com sucesso! ├в┼У┬и', 'success');
        } catch (err) {
          console.error("Import Error:", err);
          showToast(`Erro no Backup: ${err.message}`, 'error');
        } finally {
          importTimeoutRef.current = null;
        }
      }, 350); // Delay de 350ms permite que a anima├Г┬з├Г┬гo de entrada do Toast complete suavemente
    };

    reader.readAsText(file);
  }, [setAppState, showToast]);

  const handleExport = useCallback(() => {
    exportData(useAppStore.getState().appState);
    showToast('Backup exportado!', 'success');
  }, [showToast]);

  const handleCloudRestore = useCallback((d) => {
    if (d) {
      setAppState(d);
      showToast('Restaurado da Nuvem!', 'success');
    }
  }, [setAppState, showToast]);

  // BUG-06 FIX: Removed useless useMemo. It used location.pathname as dep,
  // so it re-created on every navigation ├втВмтАЭ exactly when Routes re-renders anyway.
  const routesContent = (
    <div className="animate-page-entrance">
      <ErrorBoundary>
        <Suspense fallback={
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center p-20 text-purple-400">
            <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-purple-500"></div>
          </div>
        }>
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/pomodoro" element={<Pomodoro />} />
            <Route path="/tasks" element={<Tasks />} />
            <Route path="/simulados" element={<Simulados />} />
            <Route path="/stats" element={<Stats />} />
            <Route path="/evolution" element={<Evolution />} />
            <Route path="/coach" element={<Coach />} />
            <Route path="/history" element={<History />} />
            <Route path="/sessions" element={<Sessions />} />
            <Route path="/heatmap" element={<Activity />} />
            <Route path="/retention" element={<Retention />} />
            <Route path="/notes" element={<Notes />} />
            <Route path="/flashcards" element={<Flashcards />} />
            <Route path="/agenda" element={<Agenda />} />
            <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
          </Routes>
        </Suspense>
      </ErrorBoundary>
    </div>
  );


  // ├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм Render Logic ├втАЭтВм├втАЭтВм
  if (!isStoreHydrated) {
    return (
      <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-[#020617] gap-6 animate-fade-in">
        <div className="relative">
          <div className="w-20 h-20 border-4 border-indigo-500/10 border-t-indigo-500 rounded-full animate-spin" />
          <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-indigo-500/20 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-white font-black uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-sm animate-pulse">Ultra Dashboard</span>
          <span className="text-slate-500 text-[10px] uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">Iniciando Motor de Persist├Г┬кncia...</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Welcome Screen bloqueante logo ap├Г┬│s o carregamento inicial (se n├Г┬гo tiver sido mostrada nesta sess├Г┬гo)
  if (currentUser && showWelcome) {
    return <WelcomeScreen onDismiss={handleDismissWelcome} />;
  }

  return (
    <div suppressHydrationWarning className="min-h-screen text-slate-200 font-sans selection:bg-purple-500/30 relative overflow-x-hidden w-full">
      {(loading || subLoading) ? (
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center p-20 text-purple-400 min-h-screen bg-[#0f172a] animate-fade-in">
          <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-purple-500"></div>
        </div>
      ) : !currentUser ? (
        <Login />
      ) : !headerData.exists ? (
        <div className="loading-screen">Carregando Store...</div>
      ) : (
        <>
          {!isPremium ? (
            <div className="fixed inset-0 z-[99999] bg-[#0a0f1e] animate-fade-in">
              <Suspense fallback={null}>
                <Paywall user={currentUser} onLogout={logout} />
              </Suspense>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="flex flex-col lg:grid lg:grid-cols-[auto_1fr] w-full h-dvh overflow-hidden animate-page-entrance">
              <Sidebar
                onOpenHelp={() => setShowHelpGuide(true)}
                isOpen={isSidebarOpen}
                onToggle={() => setIsSidebarOpen((prev) => !prev)}
                collapsed={sidebarCollapsed}
                setCollapsed={setSidebarCollapsed}
                contests={contestsMetaList}
                activeContestId={activeContestId}
                onSwitchContest={switchContest}
                onCreateContest={createNewContest}
                onDeleteContest={deleteContest}
                onOpenTrash={() => setTrashOpen(true)}
                onCloseMobile={() => setIsSidebarOpen(false)}
              />

              <div className="flex flex-col h-dvh w-full min-w-0 relative">
                <Header
                  user={headerData.user}
                  settings={headerData.settings}
                  contests={contestsMetaList}
                  activeContestId={activeContestId}
                  onSwitchContest={switchContest}
                  onCreateContest={createNewContest}
                  onDeleteContest={deleteContest}
                  onUndo={handleUndo}
                  onCloudRestore={handleCloudRestore}
                  onUpdateName={updateUserName}
                  currentData={EMPTY_OBJECT}
                  cloudStatus={cloudStatusHeader}
                  onExport={handleExport}
                  onImport={handleImport}

                  onToggleSidebar={() => setIsSidebarOpen((prev) => !prev)}
                  sidebarCollapsed={sidebarCollapsed}
                  setSidebarCollapsed={setSidebarCollapsed}
                  onOpenTrash={() => setTrashOpen(true)}
                />

                <TrashModal isOpen={trashOpen} onClose={() => setTrashOpen(false)} />

                <main className="flex-1 w-full px-4 sm:px-8 lg:px-10 mt-0 pt-[110px] lg:pt-0 pb-24 lg:pb-12 overflow-y-auto overflow-x-hidden custom-scrollbar relative z-0">
                  <Motion.div 
                    key={`${activeContestId}-${location.pathname}`} 
                    initial={{ opacity: 0.9, y: 4 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.2, ease: "easeOut" }}
                  >
                    {routesContent}
                  </Motion.div>
                </main>
                <HelpGuide isOpen={showHelpGuide} onClose={() => setShowHelpGuide(false)} />
                <OnboardingTour />
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {levelUpData && (
            <LevelUpToast
              key={levelUpData.level}
              level={levelUpData.level}
              title={levelUpData.title}
              onClose={clearLevelUp}
            />
          )}

          {/* Global Event Driven Toast Container */}
          <div className="fixed bottom-4 right-4 z-[100000] flex flex-col gap-2 pointer-events-none">
            {toasts.map((toast) => (
              <div key={toast.id} className="pointer-events-auto">
                <Toast
                  toast={toast}
                  onClose={() => removeToast(toast.id)}
                />
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <MainLayout />
    </Router>
  );
}

export default App;

// File: D:\Downloads\ultra-patched\src\components\ActivityHeatmap.jsx

import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
import { format, startOfMonth, endOfMonth, eachDayOfInterval, getDay, subMonths, addMonths } from 'date-fns';
import { ptBR } from 'date-fns/locale';
import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, Info } from 'lucide-react';
import { normalizeDate, formatDuration, getDateKey } from '../utils/dateHelper';

function ActivityHeatmap({ studyLogs = [] }) {
    const [monthOffset, setMonthOffset] = React.useState(0);


    const currentMonth = useMemo(() => {
        const base = new Date();
        return monthOffset < 0 ? subMonths(base, Math.abs(monthOffset)) :
            monthOffset > 0 ? addMonths(base, monthOffset) : base;
    }, [monthOffset]);

    const calendarData = useMemo(() => {
        const start = startOfMonth(currentMonth);
        const end = endOfMonth(currentMonth);
        const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start, end });

        const studyMap = {};
        const logsArray = Array.isArray(studyLogs) ? studyLogs : Object.values(studyLogs || {});
        logsArray.forEach(log => {
            const rawDate = normalizeDate(log?.date);
            if (!rawDate) return;
            const dateKey = getDateKey(rawDate) || format(rawDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
            const minutes = Math.max(0, Number(log?.minutes) || 0);
            studyMap[dateKey] = (studyMap[dateKey] || 0) + minutes;
        });

        const weeks = [];
        let currentWeek = [];

        const startDay = getDay(start);
        for (let i = 0; i < startDay; i++) {
            currentWeek.push(null);
        }

        const today = getDateKey(new Date()) || format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');

        days.forEach(day => {
            const dateKey = getDateKey(day) || format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
            const minutes = studyMap[dateKey] || 0;

            currentWeek.push({
                date: day,
                dateKey,
                minutes,
                isToday: dateKey === today,
                level: minutes === 0 ? 0 :
                    minutes < 30 ? 1 :
                        minutes < 60 ? 2 :
                            minutes < 120 ? 3 : 4
            });

            if (currentWeek.length === 7) {
                weeks.push(currentWeek);
                currentWeek = [];
            }
        });

        if (currentWeek.length > 0) {
            while (currentWeek.length < 7) {
                currentWeek.push(null);
            }
            weeks.push(currentWeek);
        }

        const totalDays = days.length;
        const monthKeys = new Set(days.map(day => getDateKey(day) || format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd')));
        const studiedDays = days.filter(day => {
            const dateKey = getDateKey(day) || format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
            return studyMap[dateKey] > 0;
        }).length;
        const totalMinutes = Object.entries(studyMap)
            .filter(([key]) => monthKeys.has(key))
            .reduce((acc, [, mins]) => acc + mins, 0);

        const totalTimeStr = formatDuration(totalMinutes / 60);

        return { weeks, totalDays, studiedDays, totalMinutes, totalTimeStr };
    }, [currentMonth, studyLogs]);

    const levelColors = [
        'bg-slate-800/40 border-white/5',
        'bg-emerald-900/40 border-emerald-800/50',
        'bg-emerald-600/50 border-emerald-500/50',
        'bg-emerald-500/80 border-emerald-400/80 shadow-[0_0_10px_rgba(16,185,129,0.3)]',
        'bg-emerald-400 border-emerald-300 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(16,185,129,0.6)] font-bold text-emerald-900',
    ];

    const weekDays = ['Dom', 'Seg', 'Ter', 'Qua', 'Qui', 'Sex', 'S├Г┬бb'];

    return (
        <div className="w-full max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6 border-b border-white/10 pb-4">
                <div className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-widest flex items-center gap-2">
                    <span className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-emerald-500 animate-pulse"></span>
                    Vis├Г┬гo Mensal
                    <div className="relative group/tooltip cursor-help ml-1 inline-flex">
                        <Info size={14} className="text-slate-500/50 hover:text-slate-400 transition-colors" />
                        <div className="absolute top-full left-0 mt-2 w-56 p-2 bg-yellow-400 text-[10px] text-slate-900 rounded-lg shadow-xl opacity-0 invisible group-hover/tooltip:opacity-100 group-hover/tooltip:visible transition-all duration-300 z-[60] pointer-events-none border border-yellow-500 font-normal tracking-normal normal-case">
                            <strong>Mapa de Calor:</strong> Cada quadrado representa um dia. Quanto mais escuro o verde, mais tempo de estudo foi registrado no cron├Г┬┤metro ou adicionado manualmente.
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <button
                        onClick={() => setMonthOffset(m => Math.max(-24, m - 1))}
                        disabled={monthOffset <= -24}
                        className="p-2 rounded-xl hover:bg-white/10 text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-all border border-transparent hover:border-white/10"
                    >
                        <ChevronLeft size={18} />
                    </button>
                    <span className="text-base font-black text-white min-w-[120px] text-center capitalize tracking-tight">
                        {format(currentMonth, 'MMMM yyyy', { locale: ptBR })}
                    </span>
                    <button
                        onClick={() => setMonthOffset(m => Math.min(0, m + 1))}
                        disabled={monthOffset >= 0}
                        className="p-2 rounded-xl hover:bg-white/10 text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-all border border-transparent hover:border-white/10 disabled:opacity-30 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
                    >
                        <ChevronRight size={18} />
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2 mb-3">
                {weekDays.map(day => (
                    <div key={day} className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 text-center font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">
                        {day}
                    </div>
                ))}
            </div>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2">
                {calendarData.weeks.flatMap((week, weekIndex) =>
                    week.map((day, dayIndex) => (
                        <div
                            key={`${weekIndex}-${dayIndex}`}
                            tabIndex={day ? 0 : -1}
                            role={day ? 'button' : undefined}
                            aria-label={day ? `${Math.round(Number(day.minutes) || 0)} minutos estudados em ${format(day.date, "dd 'de' MMMM", { locale: ptBR })}` : 'Sem dados de estudo'}
                            className={`
                                w-full aspect-square rounded-xl md:rounded-2xl border transition-all duration-300 cursor-default group relative focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400
                                ${day ? levelColors[day.level] : 'bg-transparent border-transparent'}
                                ${day?.isToday ? 'ring-2 ring-emerald-500 ring-inset z-10' : ''}
                                ${day ? 'hover:scale-110 hover:z-20 hover:border-white/50' : ''}
                            `}
                        >
                            {day && (
                                <div className={`absolute bottom-full mb-3 px-4 py-3 bg-slate-900/95 backdrop-blur-xl border border-white/10 rounded-xl shadow-2xl text-center whitespace-nowrap opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-300 pointer-events-none z-50 transform translate-y-2 group-hover:translate-y-0 focus-within:opacity-100 focus-within:translate-y-0 ${dayIndex === 0 ? 'left-[-10px]' : dayIndex === 6 ? 'right-[-10px]' : 'left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2'}`}>
                                    <div className={`absolute -bottom-2 w-4 h-4 bg-slate-900 border-b border-r border-white/10 rotate-45 ${dayIndex === 0 ? 'left-6' : dayIndex === 6 ? 'right-6' : 'left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2'}`}></div>
                                    <p className="relative z-10 text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-bold capitalize mb-1 tracking-widest">{format(day.date, "dd 'de' MMMM (EEEE)", { locale: ptBR })}</p>
                                    <p className="relative z-10 text-sm font-black text-white">
                                        {day.minutes > 0
                                            ? <span className="text-emerald-400">{formatDuration(day.minutes / 60)}</span>
                                            : 'Descanso'}
                                    </p>
                                </div>
                            )}
                        </div>
                    ))
                )}
            </div>

            <div className="mt-8 pt-6 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-center justify-between gap-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-slate-900/50 px-4 py-2 rounded-full border border-white/5">
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Menos</span>
                    <div className="flex gap-1.5 mx-2">
                        {levelColors.map((color, i) => (
                            <div key={i} className={`w-4 h-4 rounded-md border ${color.split(' ')[0]} ${color.split(' ')[1]}`} />
                        ))}
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Mais</span>
                </div>

                <div className="flex items-center gap-4 bg-slate-900/50 px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl border border-white/5">
                    <div className="text-center">
                        <div className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-widest mb-0.5">Dias Ativos</div>
                        <div className="text-sm text-slate-300"><span className="text-emerald-400 font-black">{calendarData.studiedDays}</span> / {calendarData.totalDays}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="w-px h-8 bg-white/10"></div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                        <div className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-widest mb-0.5">Tempo Total</div>
                        <div className="text-sm text-white font-black">{calendarData.totalTimeStr}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
}

export default React.memo(ActivityHeatmap);

import React, { useState, useMemo, useEffect } from 'react';
